# CoralOS тАФ Live Board v2
> Reset 2026-06-04 from Florin's full "state of the union" walkthrough of the deployed app.
> **This file is now the active tracker.** `pro-hardening.md` is archived history (many items there were marked done but are shallow/broken in production тАФ do NOT trust its statuses; THIS board is ground truth).
> North star: **FINANCIAL CORRECTNESS first.** Sequencing: **FOUNDATION-FIRST** (fix shared primitives that cause many symptoms before chasing individual symptoms).

---

## ЁЯФТ EXECUTION PROTOCOL (binding тАФ the trust reset)
1. **ONE workstream item at a time.** Complete it, STOP. No multi-item commits.
2. **Two-stage status, Florin gates.** Coder may reach `ЁЯЯв DONE тАФ awaiting verify` (the furthest the coder goes). ONLY Florin sets `тЬЕ VERIFIED`. **No new item starts until the current one is `тЬЕ VERIFIED`.** Failed verify тЖТ `ЁЯЯб IN PROGRESS` тЖТ fix тЖТ resubmit.
3. **Commit naming = checksum.** One item = one commit: `<ITEM-ID>: <short imperative>` (e.g. `FIN-1: credit-note links by parentInvoiceId only`). Same ID on follow-ups. No creative/bundled names. So `git log --oneline` is glanceable against this board.
4. **Measure, don't claim.** "Done" = you tested the real behavior on the deploy and stated HOW in feedback. "Implemented" тЙа done.
5. **Regression rule.** An increment must not break anything previously `тЬЕ VERIFIED`. If it does тЖТ it's not done.
6. **Branch:** all work on `develop`; promote to `main` + tag only at version checkpoints (below).
7. **SEPARATION OF POWERS (binding тАФ prevents lost-update clobbers).** `board-v2.md` is the **Planner's file ONLY**. The **coder must NEVER edit `board-v2.md`** (no "docs: update board" commits) тАФ its status channel is the deterministic `TASK-ID:` commit name (rule 3), which IS how it reports. The **Planner** owns the board and reconciles the commit log into it. **Florin** screenshots the board for the human view and cross-checks against `git log --oneline`. Two writers on one file = silent lost updates (happened 2026-06-07: coder commits reverted Planner edits). One writer per artifact.

---

## ЁЯЯв HAPPY PATH (the spine тАФ every increment must move a real user one verified step further)
FREE tier тЖТ first paid:
**signup тЖТ company data correct & stable тЖТ create invoice (engine usable) тЖТ send invoice (email works) тЖТ log expense (scan stores file) тЖТ receive Peppol (SMP live) тЖТ accountant export.**
Financial correctness underpins the middle of this path тЖТ that's why FIN workstream goes first.

### ЁЯЪА FREE-TIER LAUNCH READINESS (Planner audit 2026-06-18 тАФ features mostly EXIST; blockers are RELIABILITY, not missing features)
Per-step real status (code-inspected). **Launch blockers = the тЫФ rows.**
1. **Signup тЖТ company data stable** тАФ тЬЕ exists; PROFILE-2 committed (numbering/branding persistence). PROFILE-3-stationery = polish, not a blocker.
2. **Create invoice (engine usable)** тАФ тЬЕ engine exists (`ClientInvoiceEngine`, AGG done). тЫФ **GRID-12** (typing lands in the wrong record) corrupts data entry across clients/suppliers/invoices тЖТ **must fix before launch**. тЫФ **FIN-7b-APPLY** (per-tenant numbering db push) тЖТ financial correctness.
3. **Send invoice (email works)** тАФ тЬЕ works. SEND-3 (bcc/replyTo) **Planner-verified by inspection** (both `send-quote.ts` + `send-invoice.ts` L78-79). SEND-5b (public link) committed+verified. FIN-9 (legal block above totals, `wrap={false}`) **Planner-verified by inspection** (`InvoicePDFTemplate` L374/615, `QuotationPDFTemplate` L383/577; legal renders before totals) тЖТ done, NOT a blocker. SEND-6 (compose modal) = nice-to-have, NOT a blocker.
4. **Log expense (scan stores file)** тАФ тЬЕ SCAN-* committed (PDF accept, unpdf, manual capture, Blob store). DRIVE-OUT-1 (stop empty-folder spam) = hygiene.
5. **Receive Peppol (SMP live)** тАФ PEPPOL_RECEIVE is FREE-tier (confirmed `feature-flags.ts`). тЫФ **PEPPOL-4-FIX-C committed but will FAIL verify until PI-3** тАФ the UBL parser `parseFloat`s attributed amount elements тЖТ NaN, so totals/prices are still wrong. **PI-3 is part of making receive actually work.** Then Florin's live `?debug=1` check. Plus PI-1/2/4-9 for a usable inbound invoice.
6. **Accountant export** тАФ тЬЕ a `journal` module + an accountant CSV export (with `accountantExportedAt` stamping) EXIST. тЪая╕П **ASSESS-WITH-FLORIN:** is the CSV a *usable* accountant handover (structured sales+purchase journals w/ VAT base per rate), or just a raw property dump? Likely needs a proper "Boekhouder export" (sales journal + purchase journal + PDF zip for a date range). NOT building blind тАФ needs Florin's format call. **No code until decided.**
**тЗТ Free-tier launch blockers (FIN-9 + SEND-3 now Planner-verified done, removed): GRID-12 (data corruption), PI-3 (inbound totals/prices NaN тАФ makes PEPPOL receive actually correct), FIN-7b-APPLY (numbering db push), PEPPOL-4-FIX-C verify (Florin live check, after PI-3), and the accountant-export assessment (Florin format call). PI-1/PI-2 (download + manual-edit safety net) are quick high-value adjacents. Everything else in the queue (NOTIF-*, PROJ-8/9/10 Kanban, GRID-2/3/4/5/9 cosmetics, CROSS-1, GRID-9b, GRID-13a drop-indicator, SEND-6, DRIVE-OUT-2/3/4) is POST-launch тАФ coder clears the 4 blockers first.**

## ЁЯФв VERSION CHECKPOINTS (a tag = "everything up to here works, nothing prior regressed")
- **v0.1 тАФ Financial core correct.** FIN workstream fully тЬЕ: invoice/credit-note correctness, numbering, sent-doc edit-lock exemption, credited %. The money is trustworthy.
- **v0.2 тАФ Database foundation solid.** GRID workstream тЬЕ: editing no longer janky, flyouts edge-safe, detail-views removed app-wide, selects searchable. The app stops feeling half-broken.
- **v0.3 тАФ Real editor + blocks.** EDITOR workstream тЬЕ: Notion-grade rich text everywhere it's needed.
- **v0.4 тАФ Free-tier happy path.** CaptureтЖТinvoiceтЖТsendтЖТexpenseтЖТreceiveтЖТexport all verified on mobile + desktop. **Launchable free tier.**
- **v0.5+ тАФ Modules deepened** (Projects, Inbox, Calendar, Files, Sales) + localization complete.
- Patch bumps (v0.x.N) for the cosmetic/isolated tail.

## тЪб CODER тАФ UNATTENDED QUEUE (cron-triggered)
**PER-RUN STEPS (do IN THIS ORDER every cron window):**
0. **PERSIST THE BOARD FIRST (fixes the lost-update clobber тАФ Planner edits live only in the working tree and your later `git checkout` wipes them).** Run `git status --porcelain .agents/workflows/board-v2.md`. If it reports changes, IMMEDIATELY `git add .agents/workflows/board-v2.md && git commit -m "docs(planner): persist board"` тАФ BEFORE reading the queue or touching code. You are NOT authoring/editing the board (Rule 6 still forbids that); you are only SAVING the Planner's pending edits so step 3's revert can't destroy them. This is the ONLY board commit you ever make, and it must change nothing in the file's content.
1. Read the board; take the FIRST not-yet-committed QUEUE item (top to bottom).
2. Do ONLY that item. Never expand scope.
3. `tsc` + lint must be green. If your code change breaks them and you can't fix in-window тЖТ `git checkout .` (now safe: the board was already persisted in step 0). Do NOT commit broken code.
4. Commit the code as exactly `<ID>: <imperative>` (rule 3). One item = one commit.
5. **LOOP тАФ do NOT stop after one item (the cron may only fire once, so keep working).** Go back to step 0 and take the NEXT uncommitted item. Re-read the board EVERY iteration тАФ the Planner edits it between your commits, so the top of the queue is authoritative each loop (a new ЁЯФ┤ item may have jumped ahead). Keep going, one-item-one-commit, until EITHER (a) the queue has no uncommitted items left above the `тФАтФА SUPERVISED LINE тФАтФА`, OR (b) you reach your time/compute budget for this window. Only THEN stop.
6. **CHECK-IN before stopping:** when you do stop (queue dry or budget reached), leave the working tree CLEAN (all commits made or reverted, board persisted). If you stopped because the queue is dry, your last action is simply to stop and wait for the next cron тАФ the Planner will have refilled the board by then. If the same item failed `tsc`/lint twice in a row, SKIP it permanently this session (don't loop forever on one broken item) and move on.
(Bootstrap note for Florin: commit this protocol change ONCE; from then on the coder self-persists the board each run AND loops through multiple items per fire.)

**UNATTENDED SAFETY PROTOCOL (binding):**
- **One item = one commit** named exactly `<ID>: <imperative>`. Do ONLY that item per commit тАФ never bundle. After committing, LOOP to the next item (PER-RUN steps 5тАУ6); do NOT stop after a single item. Stop only when the queue is dry (above the SUPERVISED LINE) or your window budget is spent.
- **tsc + lint must be green before committing.** If your change breaks them and you can't fix in-window тЖТ `git checkout .` (revert) and leave it; do NOT commit broken code.
- **If an item is ambiguous, needs a decision, or its files are mid-change тЖТ SKIP it, move to the next.** Never guess on scope. Never expand scope.
- **NEVER EDIT/AUTHOR `board-v2.md` content** (Planner-only, pd.md rule 6) тАФ no rewording, no status changes, no marking тЬЕ (only Florin sets тЬЕ). The ONE allowed board git action is the **content-preserving persist commit in PER-RUN STEP 0** (saving the Planner's pending edits verbatim). Report your own work only via `<ID>:` commit names.
- Items below the `тФАтФА SUPERVISED LINE тФАтФА` are OFF-LIMITS unattended (need Florin) тАФ do not start them.

**QUEUE (in order):**

## тЫФ HARD RULE тАФ CODER MUST NEVER TOUCH `main` (Florin directive 2026-06-26). Top-of-protocol, non-negotiable.
ЁЯЪл The coder works ONLY on `develop`. NEVER `git checkout main`/`staging`, NEVER commit/push/merge/rebase to `main` or `staging`, NEVER merge `main`/`staging` INTO `develop` (no back-merges). `main` and `staging` are FLORIN-ONLY; flow is one-way UP (`develop тЖТ staging тЖТ main`), promoted by Florin. If `develop` looks behind `main`, STOP тАФ leave it for Florin; do NOT reconcile with a back-merge. Any commit touching `main`/`staging` is a protocol violation. (This supersedes any older wording; also add to pd.md Rule 6 + the UNATTENDED SAFETY PROTOCOL.)

## ЁЯзн BRANCH-HYGIENE тАФ STOP the back-merges; one-way flow only (Florin chose "branch hygiene first" 2026-06-26). The resurrection vector for deleted code.
**Diagnosis (from a STALE local mount тАФ Florin verify on the real repo):** the mount is on `main` with un-fetched refs (this caused the "3 days ago"/lagging-commit confusion). Local shows `main..develop = 0`, `develop..main = 66`, and history has recurring **"Merge branch 'main' into develop"** back-merges. Those back-merges drag old/deleted state from `main` DOWN into `develop` тЖТ how deleted code (e.g. the old sidebar) resurfaces. **pd Rule 6 (staged pipeline) failure.**
**PROTOCOL (one-way; pin into pd.md):** `develop тЖТ staging тЖТ main`, NEVER the reverse. **The coder must NEVER `git merge main`/`staging` into `develop`, never `git checkout main`, never push `main`.** `main` is Florin-only and only RECEIVES (merges up from staging); nothing flows back down. Florin's hotfixes on main тЖТ cherry-pick onto develop (or make on develop and flow up), never a wholesale mainтЖТdevelop merge.
**ONE-TIME REMEDIATION (Florin runs тАФ Planner cannot mutate the repo):** (1) `git fetch --all`; pick the branch whose tree is KNOWN-GOOD now (verify deleted sidebar absent + today's WORKHUB present). (2) Bring the other branch to match it (fast-forward/reset, no merge commit). (3) develop = single active line for the coder; merge developтЖТstagingтЖТmain upward only. (4) Remove any tooling that auto-merges mainтЖТdevelop. **VERIFY:** clean linear `main`/`develop` relationship; no new "Merge main into develop"; deleted sidebar stays deleted.
**Coder-protocol amendment (add to UNATTENDED SAFETY PROTOCOL):** ЁЯЪл NEVER merge/rebase `main` or `staging` into `develop`; NEVER checkout/push `main`. Work only on `develop`. If `develop` looks behind `main`, STOP and leave it for Florin тАФ do NOT "fix" it with a back-merge.

### тЬЕ INV-EMAIL-TOTAL тАФ invoice email shows the EXCL-VAT amount as "TOTAL FACTURE" (Florin live 2026-06-22: invoice 2026-28 was 700тВм + 6% VAT but the client saw тВм700 тАФ should be тВм742). BILLING-CRITICAL: a client could underpay. DO FIRST. "make sure no mistakes are made anymore."
**Measured ROOT:** `ClientInvoiceEngine.tsx` L654 `const grandTotal = totals.subtotal;` тАФ `grandTotal` is the EXCL-VAT subtotal even though `calculateInvoiceTotals` returns `totalInclVAT` (and `totalVAT`) right there (`lib/invoice-totals.ts` L11-14). L745 sends the email with `` `тВм${grandTotal.toFixed(2)}` `` тЖТ the email's "TOTAL FACTURE" = тВм700 (excl), wrong (should be тВм742 incl). The STORED record is correct (L1744-1746 persist `totalExVat`/`totalVat`/`totalIncVat`) тАФ this is purely a DISPLAY/email defect. `grandTotal` (=subtotal) is ALSO passed as a prop to PDF/totals sub-components (L702/783/1589/1634), so the same excl-as-total mislabel likely affects the PDF and possibly the public viewer. **FIX (immediate + audit тАФ billing correctness):**
- **(1) Email NOW:** L745 must send the INCL-VAT total тАФ pass `totals.totalInclVAT.toFixed(2)` (or the stored `totalIncVat`). The email header "TOTAL FACTURE / Total" MUST be VAT-inclusive (= amount due). `totalInclVAT` already handles reverse-charge/medecontractant correctly (equals subtotal when VAT=0), so it's right in all cases.
- **(2) Audit every CLIENT-FACING total** (pd Rule 2, measure each): the PDF totals block, the public `InvoiceViewer` "montant d├╗"/total, and the engine headline. Each must show **Subtotal (excl/HT) тЖТ VAT per rate тЖТ TOTAL (incl/montant d├╗)**, with the headline/amount-due = `totalInclVAT`. The mis-named `grandTotal=subtotal` should be split: pass explicit `grandTotalExcl` AND `grandTotalIncl` (+ `vatAmount`) to sub-components and label each correctly тАФ do NOT blindly flip `grandTotal` everywhere (a place that legitimately shows the excl subtotal must keep it, just labeled "excl/HT"). The public InvoiceViewer currently shows `total_excl` columns (L113) тАФ confirm it also shows the VAT + incl total prominently.
- **(3) Same check for QUOTES** (`ClientQuotationEngine` + quote email/PDF/viewer) тАФ verify the client-facing total is incl-VAT too, so the same class of error can't exist there.
**VERIFY:** re-send the 700 + 6% case тЖТ the email, the PDF, and the public viewer all show **тВм742.00** as the total/amount due (with тВм700 excl + тВм42 VAT broken out); a reverse-charge invoice shows excl=incl with the medecontractant note; quotes likewise. **Commit:** `INV-EMAIL-TOTAL: client-facing invoice/quote total is VAT-inclusive (email+pdf+viewer)`.

### ~~ЁЯФ┤ЁЯФ┤ JOURNAL-SOURCE-FIX~~ тАФ COMMITTED `a851944` (Planner audit 2026-06-26 #120). Journal reads from linked entries only, never the record's own blocks. Awaiting Florin verify: open a quote's Journal тЖТ ZERO quote lines shown; add a note тЖТ quote lines/totals unchanged; entries survive reload.
**Measured ROOT (`JournalCard.tsx`):** `allDisplayBlocks = [...contentBlocks, ...linkedBlocks]` (L181) where `contentBlocks = page.blocks` (L169/172) тАФ the RECORD'S OWN blocks. On a quote, `page.blocks` ARE the quote's financial-row lines тЖТ each renders as a "journal entry." AND `handleAddQuickEntry` (L183-197) writes the new entry INTO `page.blocks` via `updatePageBlocks(databaseId, pageId, [newBlock, ...existing])` тЖТ adding a journal note to a quote POLLUTES the quote's content/lines. The CORRECT source already exists: `linkedJournalEntries` from `db-journal-general` filtered by `linkedRecordId===pageId && linkedDatabaseId===databaseId` (L154-159). **FIX:** (1) display ONLY linked journal entries тАФ `allDisplayBlocks = linkedBlocks`; DROP `contentBlocks` entirely (a record's own blocks are NEVER journal entries). (2) `handleAddQuickEntry` must CREATE A LINKED JOURNAL PAGE in `db-journal-general` (`createPage` with props `linkedRecordId=pageId`, `linkedDatabaseId=databaseId`, `author`, `createdAt`, and the entry as `initialBlocks`) тАФ NOT touch the record's `page.blocks`. (3) inline edit/delete operate on the LINKED journal page's blocks, not the record's. **VERIFY:** open a QUOTE's Journal тЖТ ZERO quote lines shown, only real journal entries; add an entry тЖТ a journal entry is created and the quote's lines/totals are UNCHANGED; same for project/record; entries persist in `db-journal-general` and survive reload. **Commit:** `JOURNAL-SOURCE-FIX: journal uses only linked entries, never the record's own blocks`.

### ЁЯФ┤ SELECT-LINGER тАФ SearchableSelect won't close on outside click; it lingers (Florin live 2026-06-25: "selects open and are so difficult to close backтАж otherwise it lingers"). Regression-companion to SELECT-MODAL-DISMISS.
**Measured ROOT (`SearchableSelect.tsx`):** the close-on-outside-click handler (L74-87) attaches `document.addEventListener('mousedown', handleClick)` in the **BUBBLE** phase. But SELECT-MODAL-DISMISS added `onMouseDown={e=>e.stopPropagation()}` to the portaled dropdown (L141-142), and MANY other components (other portaled selects, menus, grid cells, dialog chrome) also stop `mousedown` propagation тЖТ an outside click on any such element never bubbles up to `document`, so `handleClick` never fires and the dropdown stays open ("lingers"). The only way to close is to click an element that happens NOT to stop propagation (Florin's three-dot-menu тЖТ outside sequence). **FIX:** attach the outside-click listener in the **CAPTURE** phase тАФ `document.addEventListener('mousedown', handleClick, true)` (and `removeEventListener(..., true)`). Capture runs BEFORE any bubble-phase `stopPropagation`, and `handleClick` already checks containment (`containerRef`/`dropdownRef`), so clicks INSIDE the select still don't close it while clicks ANYWHERE outside now do. Also add **Escape closes** (`keydown` Esc тЖТ `setIsOpen(false)`). The SELECT-MODAL-DISMISS guard (dropdown clicks not closing the parent dialog) is unaffected тАФ it's about the parent's listener, not this one. **VERIFY:** open a SearchableSelect тЖТ click anywhere outside (incl. another select, a menu, a grid cell, dialog chrome) тЖТ it closes immediately; clicking the search field / an option does NOT close prematurely; Esc closes; in the Schedule New Shift dialog the parent modal still does NOT close when interacting with the select (SELECT-MODAL-DISMISS holds). **Commit:** `SELECT-LINGER: capture-phase outside-click close + Esc (immune to stopPropagation)`.

### ~~ЁЯЯа PORTAL-MULTI-PROJECT~~ тАФ COMMITTED `37f64b9`
**State:** `37f64b9` тЬЕ DONE (2026-06-27)
**Why:** A single client often has multiple projects (e.g., multiple renovations for one investor, or a master agreement). One portal should serve the *Client*, listing their active projects.

**Phase 1 (Data & API)**:
- `ClientPortal` model removes hard dependency on one project, resolves via dynamic relation (e.g. `clientEmail` or `clientId` relation).
- Portal fetch resolves ALL projects linked to that client in the `db-1` database.
- Schema updated: `projectId` added to `Document`, `ProjectMedia`, `Message`, and `ProjectUpdate` to isolate them per-project instead of per-portal.

**Phase 2 (UI)**:
- Portal landing is a PROJECT LIST if > 1 project. Selecting one opens details.
- Single-project clients auto-open directly to details.
- Media, Documents, Tasks, and Messages are scoped to the selected project.

**Phase 3 (Admin)**:
- `/admin/portals` handles creation linking (can link multiple or just leave it at client-level).

**Status:** Completed `37f64b9`.

### ЁЯЯб SEND-PWA-CAPTURE тАФ installed CoralOS PWA hijacks the emailed quote link on desktop (Planner 2026-06-22, Florin live: "launches coralOS to view and sign; i have to right-click тЖТ open withтАж"). NOT client-facing-blocking тАФ flagged lower; needs care (touches manifest + routing).
**Measured root:** `public/manifest.json` (`scope:"/"`, start_url `/admin/dashboard`) and `public/manifest-workhub.json` (`scope:"/"`) make the installed PWA capture the ENTIRE origin тЖТ on a machine where CoralOS is installed, a public `/{locale}/quote/тАж` (or `/invoice/тАж`) link deep-links into the APP window instead of the browser. **A real client (no PWA installed) is UNAFFECTED тАФ they get the browser; mobile already correct.** So this only bites tenants who installed the app (e.g. Florin testing). **Why it's fiddly:** a manifest `scope` is a single path prefix and CANNOT exclude a sub-path, and the app's routes are locale-prefixed (`/nl/admin`, `/fr/admin`тАж) so there's no clean app-only prefix to scope to. **MEASURE-FIRST, then pick (Florin to weigh in):** (a) narrow the installed-app `scope`/`start_url` if a prefix exists that covers the app surface but NOT `/quote|/invoice` (likely not, given locale prefixes) тАФ investigate; (b) **bulletproof option:** serve the public quote/invoice viewers from a host with no PWA (e.g. the marketing/`www` host or a dedicated `sign.coral-group.be`) so those links ALWAYS open in the browser тАФ bigger change, touches the email link builder (`send-quote.ts`/`send-invoice.ts`) + routing; (c) try the `launch_handler`/`capture_links` manifest hints (limited browser support) as a lightweight mitigation; (d) accept + document if none is clean, since clients are unaffected. **Do NOT guess-change the manifest scope and risk breaking the installed app's routing тАФ REPRODUCE + measure which option holds.** **VERIFY:** on a machine with CoralOS installed, clicking an emailed quote link opens the DEFAULT BROWSER public signing page, not the app window; the installed app still launches/route correctly from its own icon. **Commit (per chosen path):** `SEND-PWA-CAPTURE: public viewer links open in browser not installed PWA`.

### ~~ЁЯФ┤ SELECT-MODAL-DISMISS~~ тАФ COMMITTED `1c4156b` (Planner audit 2026-06-27 cron; duplicate of struck entry line 233). ~~SearchableSelect inside a dialog closes the modal when you click its search (Planner 2026-06-22, Florin live: "search is unclickable, it closes the modal" тАФ Schedule New Shift тЖТ Project). Regression introduced by SELECT-PORTAL; component-level fix.
**ROOT (measured):** SELECT-PORTAL made `src/components/ui/SearchableSelect.tsx` portal its dropdown to `document.body` (`createPortal`, `fixed z-[99999]`, L138-190) тАФ correct for un-clipping. BUT the portaled wrapper (L141) does NOT stop pointer-event propagation. The Schedule New Shift modal is a Radix `Dialog`/`DialogContent` (`CreateShiftForm.tsx` uses `SearchableSelect` for Project; rendered by `EditShiftDialog`/the shadcn Dialog). Because the dropdown DOM lives OUTSIDE the `DialogContent` subtree, Radix's DismissableLayer sees a pointerdown on the search input/options as an OUTSIDE interaction тЖТ fires `onOpenChange(false)` тЖТ the whole modal closes before the click lands. So the search appears "unclickable." **FIX (in `SearchableSelect.tsx`, component-level = Rule 7, repairs EVERY SearchableSelect inside any Radix Dialog/Popover):** add `onPointerDown={(e)=>e.stopPropagation()}` AND `onMouseDown={(e)=>e.stopPropagation()}` to the portaled dropdown container (L141) so interactions inside the dropdown don't bubble to `document` and trip an ancestor dismissable layer's outside-close. Keep the existing inner option/clear `stopPropagation` and the keyboard handling; do NOT remove the portal (it's what fixes SELECT-PORTAL clipping тАФ only stop the events). **VERIFY:** Schedule New Shift тЖТ open Project тЖТ click the search field + type тЖТ modal STAYS open, list filters, picking a project works and the dropdown still escapes container clipping; a SearchableSelect NOT in a dialog (engine/project dashboard) still works unchanged. **Commit:** `SELECT-MODAL-DISMISS: stop dropdown pointer events from closing parent dialog`.

**PI-FIX тАФ Purchase-Invoice engine + inbound parser (Florin 2026-06-18, 8 bugs). VAT-relevant (inbound invoices still wrong). Files: `PurchaseInvoiceEngine.tsx`, `lib/e-invoice-inbox.ts` (parser), `api/peppol/inbox/route.ts`. Do PI-3 + PI-1 + PI-2 FIRST (worst data + the manual-fix safety net).**
- **PI-3 (ROOT-CAUSE, do first) тАФ line prices/qty + header totals all parse to NaN.** `parseUBLToInvoice` config `ignoreAttributes:false` тЖТ UBL amount elements carry attributes (`<PriceAmount currencyID="EUR">12.50</PriceAmount>`, `InvoicedQuantity unitCode=тАж`) so fast-xml-parser yields `{'#text':'12.50','@_currencyID':'EUR'}`. Then `parseFloat(line.Price?.PriceAmount)`, `parseFloat(line.LineExtensionAmount)`, `parseFloat(line.InvoicedQuantity)`, `parseFloat(legalTotal.TaxExclusiveAmount/PayableAmount)`, `TaxAmount` ALL `parseFloat` an OBJECT тЖТ **NaN** (this is why prices AND totals are wrong even after FIX-C). **FIX:** add helper `const num = (v:any)=>{const s=(v&&typeof v==='object')?v['#text']:v; const n=parseFloat(String(s??'').replace(',', '.')); return isNaN(n)?0:n;}` and `const txt=(v:any)=>String((v&&typeof v==='object')?(v['#text']??''):(v??'')).trim();` Use `num()` for EVERY amount/qty/price/percent and `txt()` for names/descriptions. **Both render paths share this parser** тАФ the stored `financial-row` blocks (built in the inbound route) AND the engine's "Legacy Peppol Line Items" table (fed live by `GET /api/peppol/inbox/[docId]` тЖТ `data.parsed`). So this one fix repairs both; the legacy path re-parses on open, so existing invoices show correct lines immediately (no backfill). **VERIFY (real case, Florin 2026-06-19): the BigMat Haren invoice (header тВм156.55/тВм32.88/тВм189.43 correct, but every line Price+Total = тВмNaN) тАФ after fix, reopening shows real per-line prices/totals, no NaN.** **Commit:** `PI-3: UBL numeric/text extraction handles attributed elements`.

- **ЁЯФ┤ЁЯФ┤ FIN-NUM тАФ MAJOR: document numbering ignores the tenant profile (Florin 2026-06-19 "heywire, does not respect the set profile"). ROOT CAUSE FOUND.** TWO competing numbering systems: (1) `getNextDocumentNumber` (`actions/next-document-number.ts`) тАФ CORRECT: reads the tenant profile (`{docType}Prefix/Connector/DateFormat/NumberWidth/NextNumber`), atomic, profile-respecting; used by CreateInvoice/QuotationButton. Any path that creates a db-invoices/db-quotations page WITHOUT a pre-set title falls into the hardcoded path тАФ notably the quoteтЖТinvoice conversion (`ClientQuotationEngine.handleConvertToInvoice`, comment "title is auto-numbered by store"). Result: some docs get `INV-2026-001` (profile), others `FAC-2026-001`/`CEO-2026-001.00` (hardcoded) тЖТ inconsistent, profile ignored. **FIX тАФ single source of truth = `getNextDocumentNumber`:** (a) DELETE the hardcoded numbering blocks in `store.ts` (L633-666 + L818-854) тАФ the store must NOT mint document numbers; (b) make the quoteтЖТinvoice conversion `await getNextDocumentNumber('invoice')` and pass it as `title` before/at `createPage`; (c) AUDIT every `createPage(db-invoicesтАж/db-quotationsтАж)` caller тАФ each must supply a `getNextDocumentNumber`-derived title (so nothing creates a numberless or hardcoded-numbered doc). Keep the OGM block (L670) untouched. **VERIFY:** set a custom profile (e.g. prefix `F`, format `YYYY`, width 4, connector `/`) тЖТ create an invoice via the button AND via quoteтЖТinvoice conversion тЖТ BOTH produce `F/2026/0001`-style numbers matching the profile, sequential, no `FAC`/`CEO`. **Commit:** `FIN-NUM: single profile-respecting numbering source, remove store hardcoded numbers`.

Rewrite store: `fetchNodes`тЖТ`listRecordFiles`; `uploadFile`тЖТ`uploadFileAction` then refetch; `deleteNode`тЖТ`deleteFileAction`. DELETE `createFolder`/`createGoogleFile`/`initializeContextFolder`. `FileManager.tsx`: remove New-Folder + New-Google-Doc buttons; keep upload/list/delete + `node.url`. VERIFY: list/upload/delete via Blob; no `/api/drive` calls. **Commit:** `DRIVE-OUT-2: file manager store + actions on blob seam`.

## ЁЯОп AGGREGATE PLAN тАФ Purchase-Invoice Detail View + Inbound Mapping (SINGLE SPEC тАФ follow exactly, no interpretation)
**This supersedes the purchase-invoice parts of GRID-10 + PEPPOL-4. One coherent result. Reference = Florin's 2 screenshots: image 1 = the WRONG generic modal (sparse, useless); image 2 = the CORRECT full split view (BigMat).**
**TARGET RESULT:** Opening ANY purchase invoice (manual, scanned, or Peppol-inbound) shows the FULL `PurchaseInvoiceEngine` split view тАФ LEFT: all properties + **ORDERLIJNEN** (line-item table) + **BIJLAGEN** (attachments incl. source doc); RIGHT: the **original document rendered** (PDF). The generic `PageModal` is NEVER used for `db-expenses`. Inbound invoices arrive with supplier linked, line items structured, and the original document stored.

**MEASURED FACTS (don't re-investigate):**
- `expenses/invoices/page.tsx` renders `<DatabaseClone databaseId="db-expenses">` (grid) AND has `<PurchaseInvoiceEngine pageId onClose>` (L232) тАФ but the engine opens ONLY via `selectedInvoiceId`, which is set ONLY by `handleNewManual` (new manual). **Existing/inbound row-clicks fall through to DatabaseClone's internal `PageModal` (the wrong sparse modal).**
- `PurchaseInvoiceEngine.tsx` = the correct split view (image 2). It exists and works for new-manual.
- Inbound mapping in `api/peppol/inbox/route.ts` `globalPage.create` (L264-289): `supplier` relation empty unless VAT pre-matched; lines stored as `invoiceLines: JSON.stringify(...)` + first line in `betreft`; NO original document stored (`blocks:[]`, only `peppolDocId`).
- `PurchaseInvoicePDF.tsx` = the regenerated stub ("Generated by CoralOS / No line item detail") тАФ the download Florin got. Not the original.

**EXECUTE тАФ 4 parts, each its own commit:**
1. **AGG-1 тАФ Route row-clicks to PurchaseInvoiceEngine (kills the generic modal for expenses).** Add an optional `onOpenRecord?: (pageId: string) => void` prop to `DatabaseClone`; when provided, a row "open" calls it INSTEAD of opening the internal `PageModal` (leave PageModal behavior for DBs that don't pass the prop тАФ don't break others). In `expenses/invoices/page.tsx`, pass `onOpenRecord={(id) => setSelectedInvoiceId(id)}`. Result: clicking any purchase-invoice row opens `PurchaseInvoiceEngine`, never the generic modal. **Verify:** open an existing AND an inbound invoice тЖТ both show the split view, not the sparse modal.
2. **AGG-2 тАФ Inbound mapping (`api/peppol/inbox/route.ts`).** (a) Supplier: when `matchSupplier(vendorVat)` finds nothing, **auto-create the supplier contact** from `vendor_name`/`vendor_tax_id`/`vendor_address` and link it (idempotent on VAT тАФ no dupes). (b) Line items: store as the SAME structured line shape `PurchaseInvoiceEngine`'s ORDERLIJNEN reads (not a JSON string; stop dumping line text into `betreft`). (c) Original document: fetch via `getInboxDocument(apiKey, doc.id)` and STORE it on the record as an attachment (Blob/`BIJLAGEN`). **Verify:** inbound from a NEW supplier тЖТ supplier linked (FROM filled), ORDERLIJNEN populated, source doc in BIJLAGEN.
3. **AGG-3 тАФ PurchaseInvoiceEngine renders all three regions for ALL sources.** Confirm/ensure: LEFT = properties + ORDERLIJNEN (reads the structured lines from AGG-2) + BIJLAGEN; RIGHT = original document rendered (from the stored attachment). Must work for inbound, scanned, and manual. **Verify:** image-2 layout for an inbound invoice тАФ line items + original PDF both visible.
4. **AGG-4 тАФ Document action serves the ORIGINAL.** The PDF/view/download action serves the STORED original document; only fall back to the regenerated `PurchaseInvoicePDF` stub when NO original exists (and don't present the stub as the supplier's invoice). **Verify:** download on an inbound invoice = the supplier's actual document, not a CoralOS stub.

**FINAL ACCEPTANCE (all true):** inbound Peppol invoice opens in the split view (NOT the generic modal); supplier shown + linked; ORDERLIJNEN populated; original document on the right + downloadable as source; generic `PageModal` never appears for `db-expenses`. **DESIGN NOTE (Florin): dislikes intrusive centered modals тАФ the engine is a full/large split surface, not a cramped centered modal.**

- **FIN-9** ЁЯУР **PDF layout: legal text BEFORE calculation block, and NEITHER may split across pages (Florin 2026-06-09).** Files: `src/components/admin/quotations/QuotationPDFTemplate.tsx` + `src/components/admin/invoices/InvoicePDFTemplate.tsx`. **Apply to EVERY template variant + BOTH render branches** (invoice has branches ~L357 & ~L597; quotation summary ~L558 + medecontractant/VAT legal ~L384-396; t1/t3/t4) тАФ a fix to one branch that leaves others splitting = FAIL.
  1. **ORDER:** in each variant, the legal-text group (`legalText` + `footer_medecontractant_legal` + `footer_vat6_legal`/0% clause) must render IMMEDIATELY BEFORE the totals/calculation (`summaryBox`) block.   2. **NO PAGE SPLIT тАФ legal block:** wrap the entire legal-text group in a single `<View wrap={false}>`. (Currently the legal block is NOT wrap-protected тЖТ it can split.)
  3. **NO PAGE SPLIT тАФ calculation block:** wrap the WHOLE `summaryBox`/totals block in `<View wrap={false}>` (not just one row). Invoice has `wrap={false}` on a totals row (L377/L617) and quotation on L558 тАФ confirm the boundary encloses the ENTIRE calc block (subtotal тЖТ VAT breakdown тЖТ grand total), not a subset.
  4. **@react-pdf semantics:** `wrap={false}` keeps a `<View>` intact тАФ if it doesn't fit on the current page it moves wholesale to the next. Legal + calc are short, so safe. (If Florin wants legal+calc ALWAYS on the same page, wrap BOTH in ONE `wrap={false}` parent тАФ but the literal ask is each-intact, so two adjacent `wrap={false}` blocks satisfies it.)
  **VERIFY:** generate a quote AND invoice long enough to push the end across a page boundary (many line items) тЖТ in every template variant: legal text sits directly above totals, and neither the legal block nor the calc block is ever cut by the page break (each moves intact to the next page if needed). Check light + the credit-note/proforma variants too.
- **FIN-10** ЁЯй╕ **DUPLICATE-BOOKING DETECTION for financial documents (Florin 2026-06-09: "we really, really need this").** Today NO dedup exists тЖТ the same supplier invoice can be booked twice (paid/accounted twice) тАФ a serious financial-integrity hole. Worst case: an invoice arrives via **Peppol** AND is also **scanned/uploaded** manually тЖТ two records, one real bill. **Scope: PURCHASE INVOICES first** (highest risk), then receipts.
  - **IDENTITY KEY (exact-match, NOT fuzzy тАФ recurring rule):** a purchase invoice's true identity = **`supplierVat` + supplier's `invoiceNumber`**. Same pair = same document = duplicate. Corroborate with `totalInclVat` + `issueDate`. Fields already exist on the record (`supplierVat`, `invoiceNumber`, `issueDate`, `totalInclVat`). When VAT or number is missing, fall back to (`supplierName` + `total` + `issueDate`) as a WEAKER warn-only match.
  - **Shared helper** `findDuplicatePurchaseInvoice({ tenantId, supplierVat, invoiceNumber, total, issueDate, excludeId? })` тЖТ returns existing match(es), tenant-scoped. SINGLE chokepoint called from EVERY ingestion path so cross-channel dups are caught: scan/upload save (`TicketCaptureModal` invoice mode + `/api/scan`), **Peppol inbox import** (`/api/peppol/inbox`), and manual create. (Matching across Peppol + scan is the key win.)
  - **(A) PREVENTIVE тАФ at scan/upload (warn before save):** if a match exists тЖТ show a blocking confirm: "A purchase invoice from {supplier} #{invoiceNumber} for тВм{total} ({issueDate}) already exists. [View existing] [Save anyway] [Cancel]." Don't hard-block (legitimate re-issues happen) but require EXPLICIT override; default = don't duplicate.
  - **(B) DETECTIVE тАФ system finds them later:** a dedup scan that groups existing purchase invoices by identity key and flags duplicate groups тЖТ surface in the Financials module (a "possible duplicates" banner/list) + a **NOTIF** notification ("N possible duplicate invoices found"). User reviews тЖТ keep one / delete the other.
  - **NOT a hard DB unique constraint** (nulls + legitimate edge cases break it) тАФ soft detection + explicit user decision. (Optional stretch: partial unique index on `(tenantId, supplierVat, invoiceNumber)` where both non-null.)
  - **INTEGRATES:** BANK-1 (OGM payment-match breaks if duplicate invoices exist), NOTIF (detective alert), Peppol inbox (cross-channel). **VERIFY:** upload the same supplier invoice twice тЖТ 2nd warns with View/Save-anyway/Cancel; receive a Peppol invoice then scan the same one тЖТ flagged as duplicate; run the detective scan over seeded dups тЖТ groups + notifies.
- **FIN-7** ЁЯй╣ **CN-from-invoice button mints the INVOICE number as the credit-note number тАФ numbering scheme ignored.** ROOT CAUSE (measured): `ClientInvoiceEngine.tsx` `handleCreateCreditNote` (~line 346-350):
  ```
  const numResult = await getNextDocumentNumber('creditnote');
  const cnNumber = numResult.success && numResult.number ? numResult.number : `CN-${invoiceNum}`;
  ```
  The proper path calls the right action, BUT the **fallback embeds the invoice number** (`CN-${invoiceNum}`). Florin sees the invoice number тЖТ the fallback is FIRING тЖТ `getNextDocumentNumber('creditnote')` is returning `success:false` in the deploy. The action itself (`next-document-number.ts:126`) looks correct, so the failure is environmental тАФ **MEASURE it (per /pd): surface `numResult.error`** (console/toast). Strong hypothesis to check first: `creditnote*` columns missing / migration not applied on the deploy тЖТ the Prisma `select:{creditnotePrefix:true,тАж}` throws тЖТ caught тЖТ success:false. (Invoice/quotation numbering work because their columns exist.) **FIX:** (1) confirm `creditnote*` columns exist + migration ran; (2) **remove the invoice-number fallback entirely** тАФ a credit note must NEVER inherit the invoice's number. On numbering failure: abort creation with a clear error (don't mint a wrong number). This supersedes FIN-2's optimistic "CN numbering тЬЕ" тАФ that was verified on a manually-created CN, not this button path.
- **FIN-7b** ЁЯй╣ **CN numbering produces DUPLICATES + out-of-sequence (EVIDENCE: Coral outbox via peppol debug, 2026-06-07).** Two sent docs both `CN-2026-007`; sequence `006,007,008` then `025` (025 created earlier); inconsistent padding (`CN-2026-006` vs `CN-2026-23`). NOT the timestamp fallback тЖТ **max-sequence read is racing**: rapid CN creation re-reads the same max / `creditnoteNextNumber` not advanced ATOMICALLY тЖТ concurrent creates collide. **FIX:** atomic numbering (DB txn + atomic `increment` on `creditnoteNextNumber`, or `MAX(seq)+1` in a serialized txn) + **UNIQUE constraint on (tenantId, invoiceNumber)** so a collision throws not duplicates; consistent zero-padding. Legal docs MUST be unique+sequential. Verify: create several CNs rapidly тЖТ all unique, consecutive, padded. [re-added after concurrent-write clobber 2026-06-07]
- **FIN-8** ЁЯй╣ **CN-from-invoice 404s after creation (document IS created, shows in Credit Notes table).** ROOT CAUSE (confirmed): `handleCreateCreditNote` does `router.push('/admin/financials/income/credit-notes/${id}')` but **that dynamic route doesn't exist** тАФ `income/credit-notes/` has only `page.tsx` (the table), no `[id]/`. **FIX:** create `src/app/[locale]/admin/financials/income/credit-notes/[id]/page.tsx` mirroring `income/invoices/[id]/page.tsx` exactly: `return <ClientInvoiceEngine id={id} locale={locale} />;` (CNs live in `db-invoices`; the engine already handles `isCreditNote`). Verify the Credit Notes table row links also target this route. (FIN-7 + FIN-8 are both in `handleCreateCreditNote` but are distinct fixes тЖТ two commits.)

## GRID тАФ Database/editing foundation (v0.2) тАФ fixes MANY symptoms at once
- **GRID-0** ЁЯЯв DONE (working tree, uncommitted) тАФ **NotionGrid.tsx decomposition (1,689тЖТ1,237 lines).** Extracted 5 units into `database/hooks/`: `useGridColumns.tsx`, `useFilteredPages.ts`, `useVatLookup.ts`, `useExportCSV.ts` + `NotionGrid.css`. **WHY: TypeScript limits.** Project `tsc --noEmit` runs >44s (heavy); a 1.7k-line component over `react-datasheet-grid`'s generic `Column<T>` is a classic source of slow type-check / build OOM / `ts2589`/`ts2590`. Decomposition + explicit param interfaces + deliberate `Column<any,any>` at the DSG boundary shrink the inference surface тАФ the correct remedy, NOT a hack. **Planner-validated:** `useGridColumns` keeps a complete `useMemo` dep array, grid `key={databaseIdRef}` and `rowData` memo intact тЖТ GRID-1/2/3 memoization PRESERVED, low regression risk. **GATE = the build:** run `next build` / full `tsc --noEmit` тЖТ must compile clean AND show reduced type-check time/mem (that's the proof the limit is relieved). **Caution logged:** both files `eslint-disable react-hooks/preserve-manual-memoization` тАФ dep arrays are complete today (omitted store actions/setters are stable), but with that lint off a future edit could silently add a stale-closure dep and reintroduce GRID-1 edit-dropouts тЖТ add a code comment warning. **Levers if still tight:** `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=4096` for build; `skipLibCheck`/`incremental` already on; **Vercel Pro's larger build resources directly help** (ties to the Pro upgrade). Apply same recipe to the next monoliths (`ClientInvoiceEngine.tsx`).
- **GRID-1** ЁЯЯв DONE тАФ awaiting Florin verify (optimized NotionGrid column memoization and stabilized key to eliminate remounts and cell edit dropouts).
- **GRID-2** ЁЯй╣ Name-property "open" button only works when the cell is NOT selected; if selected, button dead. Fix.
- **GRID-3** ЁЯй╣ **Column resize is broken: dragging a column makes it DISAPPEAR mid-drag, then it springs back at the new width only on refresh (Florin 2026-06-12).** ROOT CAUSE (Planner-diagnosed): DUAL width source-of-truth. The floating header `<div>` (`NotionGrid.tsx` ~L792/868) is bound LIVE to `resizeOffset` state тЖТ tracks the cursor. But DataSheetGrid gets width only via the column config `minWidth` (`useGridColumns` ~L84-85) and **DSG does NOT re-flow already-mounted cell layout when only `minWidth` changes between renders** тАФ it recomputes widths on MOUNT + on its own container ResizeObserver. So mid-drag the cell column gets a bad/zero effective width (тЖТ disappears) and the correct width only lands on a REMOUNT (refresh). Header (cheap, live) and grid (no reflow) diverge тЖТ the jank. **Why prior fix failed:** it propagated the value into the `columns` prop, but it never reaches DSG's *layout* without a remount тАФ and you can't remount on resize (GRID-1 stabilized `key={databaseIdRef}` to stop edit-dropout remounts). **FIX (intent тАФ coder picks the mechanism, /pd measure first: confirm DSG cell width changes during drag vs only on remount):** drive the LIVE drag purely in CSS (direct DOM width / CSS var on the grid column container) for 60fps and zero React churn, then on release commit the width to the store ONCE and trigger DSG's own remeasure WITHOUT a key-remount (e.g. dispatch a resize so its ResizeObserver fires, or the minimal layout-invalidation DSG exposes). Unify to ONE width source so header + cells cannot diverge. **VERIFY:** drag a column тЖТ it stays visible and resizes smoothly in real time; on release the new width persists with no refresh; no remount/edit-dropout.
- **GRID-4** Remove the elastic/rubber-band drag animation at view edges тАФ just stop at the edge.
- **GRID-5** ЁЯй╣ Flyouts/dropdowns clipped at screen edge everywhere. ONE fix: edge-aware positioning (measure viewport, flip orientation when overflowing). Applies app-wide (billing card, selects, menus). (was U2 + general)
- **GRID-6** Remove the standalone **details view** app-wide; standardize on the Notion-style **modal** only. Keep open-button + drag-handle actions. Applies to: Sales, Contacts, Suppliers, Articles, Receipts, Bestek. (ONE decision, ~6 modules)
- **GRID-7** Reusable **searchable select** component (type-to-filter). Used by: Quotations (project, client, pipeline), Projects, Financials. Build once.
- **GRID-8** Filter/sort UX: sort sometimes not applied (fix); filter must adapt to property TYPE тАФ select property тЖТ show its options with is/is-not; "contains" тЖТ text field. Not always a text input.
- **GRID-9** ЁЯй╣ **Notion-style detail view тАФ text too small + low contrast for the large window (Florin 2026-06-09).** MEASURED: the detail-view components render labels/values at **9тАУ12px** (`text-[9px]`, `text-[10px]`, `text-[11px]`, `text-xs`) in **muted greys** (`text-neutral-300/400/500`, `dark:text-neutral-400/500`) inside a large modal тЖТ poor legibility. Affects ALL THREE: `src/components/admin/database/components/RecordDetailPage.tsx`, `PageModal.tsx`, `ProjectDetailView.tsx`. **FIX тАФ fundamental, not ad-hoc:** define ONE legible type+contrast scale for the detail view and apply it consistently across the three files (don't tune individual classes by hand). Target scale: **property VALUES тЙе 14px (`text-sm`/`text-base`), labels 13px, section headings 16тАУ18px; ELIMINATE every `<12px` (`text-[9/10/11px]`)** in these views. **Contrast:** labels тЖТ `text-neutral-600 dark:text-neutral-300`; values тЖТ `text-neutral-900 dark:text-neutral-100`; retire `text-neutral-300/400` for primary content (keep muted only for true hints/metadata, and even then тЙе neutral-500/dark:neutral-400). Type should feel proportionate to the large window. **VERIFY:** open a record detail (large modal) тЖТ labels and values are comfortably readable at arm's length in BOTH light + dark mode; no sub-12px text; values clearly darker/stronger than labels. (Sits with GRID-6 which routed detail views into the parent-module modal.)
- **GRID-9b** SPLIT (Florin 2026-06-17): **9b-a** = inline `@` DATE insert everywhere (no NOTIF dep) тЖТ in the unattended queue NOW. **9b-b** = `@` reminder fires a notification тЖТ AFTER NOTIF (queued post-NOTIF). NOTIF itself is now in the unattended queue (16-20). (renamed from a 2nd GRID-9 collision)
- **GRID-10** ЁЯй╣ **Projects lost their ADVANCED detail view + detail-renderer FRAGMENTATION (Florin 2026-06-12: "fixed and broken multiple times тАФ make it smooth once and for all").** ROOT CAUSE (Planner, measured): the advanced `ProjectDetailView.tsx` is rendered ONLY inside the standalone `RecordDetailPage.tsx` (L208). **GRID-6 standardized on the modal (`PageModal`) and removed standalone record pages** тЖТ project records now open in `PageModal`, which is NOT type-aware and renders only the generic property view тЖТ the advanced project view is orphaned (still in the repo, never reached). That's the "simple view survived, advanced one for projects didn't."
  - **тЪая╕П CORRECTED DIRECTION (Florin 2026-06-15, with screenshots тАФ supersedes the earlier "render in the modal" framing):** GRID-6's "remove the standalone detail view, standardize on the generic modal" was the REGRESSION. The new generic `PageModal` is "completely useless" for rich document/record types тАФ it shows a few props, no line items, no original document. **KEEP / RESTORE the OLD full detail view** for rich types. Restore the standalone rich views GRID-6 bypassed rather than re-implement them in the modal.

(Apply GRID-9 legibility in those views once.)
  - **VERIFY:** open a PROJECT тЖТ advanced ProjectDetailView; open a PURCHASE INVOICE тЖТ split view with line items + original document on the right (NOT the sparse generic modal); open a Contact тЖТ light view; PDF/download serves the ORIGINAL document, not a CoralOS-regenerated sparse one; no useless generic modal for rich types. ## SCHEMA тАФ Data integrity cleanup (v0.1) тАФ SPLIT: stop the cause, THEN clean (data-safe)
> ЁЯй╕ Root cause (Planner, code-read 2026-06-04): duplicate "Quotation"/"Contacts" DBs + stray "New Workspace"/"New Database" entries are MANUFACTURED by тЙе5 uncoordinated create paths: `provisionLockedDatabases` (intended), `pages.ts:75`, `peppol/inbox/route.ts:215`, `scan/route.ts:417` (each "create-if-missing"), and `DatabaseClone.tsx:713` + `dynamic-db/page.tsx:24` (`createDatabase('New Database'тАж)`). When `getLockedDbId` resolves a tenant's system-DB id inconsistently (bare `db-quotations` vs `db-quotations-<suffix>`), multiple paths each create тЖТ duplicates. **A pure data-clean would re-spawn duplicates immediately. Must stop the cause FIRST.**

- **SCHEMA-1a** тЬЕ VERIFIED (Planner code-confirm 2026-06-04, commit `SCHEMA-1a`): all 3 server create-paths (`pages.ts`, `peppol/inbox`, `scan`) now resolve canonical id via `getLockedDbId` BEFORE the existence check тЖТ create-only-if-missing on the SAME id (no cross-path duplication). `dynamic-db` button confirmed safe (UUID id, not system prefix). DatabaseClone uses `resolveDbId`. Tap is SHUT. ┬╖ minor note: `findUnique`-then-create (not atomic upsert) тЖТ tiny theoretical race on a brand-new tenant's first DB; acceptable, suspect here if a fresh dup ever appears.
- **SCHEMA-1b** ЁЯЯв EXECUTED LIVE 2026-06-04 тАФ тЬЕ PAGE COUNTS CONSERVED both tenants (Murgu 4тЖТ4; Coral 1250тЖТ1250). Provisioned db-payments-in/out-cmneyas2, migrated 86 payment pages intact, deleted 7 empty dups + the migrated-empty sources, Murgu 1-ticket migrated. No data loss. **тП│ Florin's ONLY remaining check: open Coral тЖТ Received Payments тЖТ confirm the 86 are VISIBLE (proves the lockedDbIds repoint resolves; conserved-in-DB тЙа visible-in-UI). If blank тЖТ lockedDbIds pointer gap (data safe, snapshot covers). Then тЬЕ.** **Dry-run report (data-safe, merge of EXISTING duplicates):**
  - Build an auditable script: per tenant, group GlobalDatabases by system-type; for each type with >1, pick canonical (the one in `lockedDbIds`, else the one with most pages), **MIGRATE all GlobalPages from duplicates into the canonical**, repoint references (`lockedDbIds`, any `databaseId` FKs), THEN trash the now-empty duplicates. Remove "New Workspace"/"New Database" garbage ONLY if confirmed empty/orphaned.
  - **MANDATORY: dry-run mode that REPORTS what it would merge/delete/migrate (counts + ids) WITHOUT executing. Florin reviews the report, THEN authorizes the live run.** Never blind-delete a DB that holds pages.
  - Acceptance: each tenant has exactly ONE of each system DB; ZERO page loss (page counts before == after, in the canonical); garbage removed; dry-run report archived in feedback.
- **SCHEMA-2** Status/option IDs canonical + consistent across engine and DB views (partially touched; verify).

> тЪая╕П Data-mutating on live tenants. 1a is safe (code only). 1b MUST dry-run тЖТ Florin-approve тЖТ execute. Two separate one-at-a-time items.

## QUOTE тАФ Quotation module (v0.3/0.4)
- **QUOTE-1** Project select тЖТ searchable (GRID-7).
- **QUOTE-2** Client select тЖТ searchable (GRID-7).

- **QUOTE-6** ЁЯУЛ **PAYMENT PLAN & TERMS тАФ elaborate payment module (quote + invoice).** Florin 2026-06-08: build this properly; OGM is ALREADY done (Stripe + QR + `lib/ogm.ts` + structuredComm + `lib/dunning.ts`) тЖТ **do NOT re-implement OGM/QR/payment-link/dunning; INTEGRATE with them.** One reusable `PaymentPlan` attached to the document, tenant-level defaults + per-document override. FOUR parts:
  1. **Payment method** (per doc, default from profile): bank transfer (renders IBAN/BIC), Peppol e-invoice, cash, card/Stripe link, QR. Selectable on the document.
  2. **Payment terms:** due-date model (Net X / end-of-month / fixed date / on-receipt) тАФ extends existing `defaultPaymentTermDays` (tenant). Add Belgian B2B legal clauses: statutory late-payment interest + recovery indemnity, localized NL/FR clause text (reuse `lib/dunning.ts` logic/labels тАФ don't duplicate).
  3. **Payment schedule тАФ the core (extends the old QUOTE-6 staged idea):** a schedule builder with modes: single | deposit+balance | **staged/milestone (% of total)** | fixed-amount installments | **progress billing (% completion тЖТ vorderingsstaten)**. Each stage = row: label ("Voorschot","Bij aanvang","Bij oplevering"), trigger (date/milestone/% complete), basis (% or тВм), due-offset, status (plannedтЖТinvoicedтЖТpaid). Validate schedule sums to 100%/total. **Each stage can GENERATE its staged invoice** тЖТ quote becomes parent of a series; feeds project P&L + vorderingsstaten.
  4. **Deposit / voorschot:** special first stage, tracked against final invoice, shown as deduction ("reeds gefactureerd voorschot") so the final doc reconciles.
  **MODEL:** `PaymentPlan { method, terms{dueModel,dueDays,lateClause}, schedule[{label,trigger,basis,value,dueOffset,status,generatedInvoiceId}], deposit }` on the document (OGM stays where it is). Tenant defaults in Settings (model the setup UI like the profitability card). **INTEGRATES:** FIN-6 (VAT/totals per rate), existing OGM/QR/Stripe/dunning, BANK-1 (Ponto OGM match closes the loop: staged invoice тЖТ OGM тЖТ bank feed auto-matches), insurance-claim quote structure. (was Q5; OGM/QR explicitly out of scope тАФ already shipped.)
  **тЪая╕П BUILD IN PHASES тАФ one sub-item = one commit = one Florin тЬЕ. DO NOT build it all and hide it (that's the batched anti-pattern protocol rule 1 forbids).** Coder's instinct to do the PDF last is CORRECT тАФ that's phase 6e. Each phase below is independently verifiable in-app even before the PDF exists:
  - **QUOTE-6a тАФ Data model only.** Persist `PaymentPlan { method, terms{dueModel,dueDays,lateClause}, schedule[{label,trigger,basis,value,dueOffset,status,generatedInvoiceId}], deposit }` on the document (GlobalPage property / JSON). Read+write helpers. NO UI, NO PDF. **Verify:** a plan written programmatically round-trips on a quote (inspect in DB/devtools).
  - **QUOTE-6b тАФ Tenant defaults in Settings.** Method + terms (extends `defaultPaymentTermDays`) + NL/FR legal clause text (reuse `lib/dunning.ts` labels). **Verify:** defaults save + reload (respect PROFILE-2 hydration rules тАФ no fake-default write-back).
  - **QUOTE-6c тАФ Schedule editor UI** in the quote engine (modes: single | deposit+balance | staged % | fixed installments | progress %). Validates sum=100%/total; new-doc inherits 6b defaults. NO PDF yet тАФ visible/usable in-app only. **Verify:** build each mode in UI тЖТ persists (6a) тЖТ sums validate тЖТ reopen shows it.
  - **QUOTE-6d тАФ Logic: generate staged invoices** from the plan; deposit/voorschot deduction on the final; wire to vorderingsstaten + project P&L; stage status plannedтЖТinvoicedтЖТpaid. **Verify:** generate stage invoices тЖТ amounts correct, deposit deducts on final, statuses advance.
  - **QUOTE-6e тАФ PDF rendering (LAST).** Render payment plan + terms + schedule table on quote & invoice templates, VAT per FIN-6 rule. **Verify:** generated PDF shows the schedule, due dates, deposit deduction, legal clause; matches transmitted e-invoice. тЖР this is the "keep hidden from PDF for now" part тАФ it's simply the final phase, not a hidden flag.
  **So: yes defer the PDF (6e last), but 6aтЖТ6d are SEPARATE commits each verified by Florin тАФ not one hidden mega-build.**
- **QUOTE-7** ЁЯй╣ **Save-to-Library writes the shop discount into the SUPPLIER column, not the discount column** (margin + other fields fine). ROOT CAUSE (measured тАФ recurring substring-matching failure class): `SaveToLibraryModal.tsx` `findPropId` (line 28-30) returns the first property whose name *contains* any alias. Discount aliases `['korting','remise','discount','disc','lever']` (line 37) тАФ `'lever'` is a substring of **"Leverancier"** (the supplier relation prop `prop-art-supplier`, which is defined BEFORE `prop-art-remise`/"Discount" in the articles schema, `mockData.ts:775` vs `:778`). So `propMap.discount` resolves to `prop-art-supplier` тЖТ on save (line 78) the discount % is written into the supplier relation (corrupting it) and the real Discount prop never gets it. Margin works because `['marge','margin']` can't false-positive. **FUNDAMENTAL FIX (use schema identity, not string guessing):** `db-articles` is a SYSTEM db with canonical prop ids тАФ map directly to them (`prop-art-bruto`, `prop-art-remise`, `prop-art-margin`, `prop-art-verkoop`, `prop-art-unit`, `prop-art-type`), exactly as the apply path already does (`FinancialRowRenderer.tsx:222-224`). Only fall back to name-matching for non-system custom DBs, and when doing so use EXACT name equality тАФ never partial/substring тАФ and drop the dangerous `'lever'`/`'disc'` aliases. **Also check the invoices twin** `src/components/admin/invoices/SaveToLibraryModal.tsx` for the same poisoned alias list. **Verify:** save an article with a discount тЖТ Discount column gets it, Leverancier relation untouched; reload into a quote тЖТ discount applies.
