## FILES тАФ Storage: MIGRATE Google Drive тЖТ Vercel Blob (v0.2)
**DECISION (Florin, 2026-06-06):** App is the only door to files (no external Drive browsing). **Full migration to Vercel Blob.**
**тЬЕ PREREQS SATISFIED (Florin, 2026-06-06):** PRIVATE Blob store created (`store_yhNt9hDHlPfEV3x6`); `BLOB_READ_WRITE_TOKEN` provisioned in Vercel env (values NOT in repo тАФ env only). `BLOB_WEBHOOK_PUBLIC_KEY` available but webhooks are OPTIONAL/later (not a v0.2 dep). Stream is unblocked to run AFTER v0.1 is tagged. Drive's folder model was the root of "creates a folder per item / saved-but-not-findable / scattered roots" тАФ Blob is flat key-based storage, which structurally eliminates that entire bug class. The old FILES-1/2/3 (Drive-folder patches) are RETIRED by this decision тАФ do NOT work them.
**EXECUTION ORDER (one item = one commit, тЬЕ-gated):** FILES-ISO тЖТ FILES-0 тЖТ FILES-1 тЖТ FILES-2 тЖТ FILES-3 (data migration, dry-runтЖТFlorin-approve) тЖТ FILES-4 (retire dead Drive storage) тЖТ FILES-5 (quote image picker). SCAN-4 rides on FILES-0/1.
**SCOPE BOUNDARY тАФ read before touching anything:** Migrate ONLY the file-STORAGE surface. Google **Calendar** + **Gmail** OAuth STAY (they are not storage). Do NOT remove `api/calendar/*`, `api/email/connect/google/*`, `googleToken.ts`, or shared Google OAuth token infra. Storage surface to migrate: `lib/google-drive.ts`, the file-storage parts of `lib/google-drive-oauth.ts`, `api/drive/*` (init, route, upload, list, callback, auth, migrate-f4), `components/admin/file-manager/*`, `components/admin/drive/DriveFileExplorer.tsx`, `components/admin/expenses/TicketCaptureModal.tsx`, `useScheduleAttachments`, `useProjectAttachments`, `components/portal/DocumentManager.tsx`. **Coder: measure-before-deduce (/pd) тАФ grep the real call sites first; this list is the planner's map, not gospel.**

**NORTH-STAR DESIGN тАФ adapter seam (the general measure, not 49 detail edits):** Introduce ONE storage interface and route everything through it. The DriveтЖТBlob swap then lives at a single boundary.

- **FILES-ISO** ЁЯФТ **TENANT ISOLATION тАФ read FIRST, it shapes FILES-0.** The `t_{tenantId}/` prefix is ORGANIZATION, not a security boundary. Two non-negotiables: **(1) Use a PRIVATE Blob store** (`access: 'private'`, Vercel Private Storage тАФ built for invoices/contracts; public-beta Feb 2026). Public blobs get an unguessable-but-public URL that bypasses all auth if leaked тАФ unacceptable for an ERP. **Store privacy is fixed at store creation and CANNOT be changed after тАФ Florin must create the store as private.** Private blobs have no public URL; retrieve only via SDK `get()`. **(2) Records store the KEY, never a URL.** Serve files through an authenticated route `GET /api/files/[...key]` that (a) resolves session tenantId, (b) asserts the requested key startsWith `t_{sessionTenantId}/` тАФ reject otherwise (this is the identity-check that replaces Drive's `isFolderOwnedByTenant` parent-walk; one prefix assert, fail-closed), (c) streams the blob. EVERY `get/list/delete` derives tenantId from session and refuses keys outside the prefix тАФ NEVER trust a client-supplied key. (Recurring failure class: validate identity, not the string.) **(3) ISOLATION UNIT TEST (required, Florin 2026-06-17):** add a test that asserts a session for tenant A requesting a key under `t_{tenantB}/` is REJECTED (and a valid same-tenant key passes). This proves isolation in code тАФ chosen over per-tenant Blob stores (which hit Vercel's per-plan store cap + token-per-tenant sprawl; single private store + this prefix-assert is the scalable, standard model, consistent with our single-DB tenant-scoping). **DECISION CONFIRMED (Florin 2026-06-17): single PRIVATE store + key-prefix isolation тАФ NOT store-per-tenant.**
- **FILES-0** Define `StorageProvider` interface in `src/lib/storage/index.ts`: `put(key, data, opts) тЖТ {key, url}`, `get(key) тЖТ stream/url`, `delete(key)`, `list(prefix) тЖТ entries`. Add `BlobStorageProvider` (`@vercel/blob`, **`access: 'private'`**) as the implementation. `put` returns the KEY (persist that on the record); reads go through the FILES-ISO serving route, not a stored public URL. **Key scheme (tenant-isolated, flat):** `t_{tenantId}/{recordType}/{recordId}/{filename}` (e.g. `t_ten-gar163.../receipt/pg-abc/aldi-2026-06.pdf`). No folder objects тАФ the prefix IS the namespace. **EXCEPTION тАФ projects allow subfolders:** project keys may carry an arbitrary nested subpath: `t_{tenantId}/project/{recordId}/{subpathтАж}/{filename}` (e.g. `тАж/project/pg-7/permits/2026/bouwvergunning.pdf`). Blob keys are plain slash-delimited strings, so subfolders cost nothing at storage level тАФ they are VIRTUAL, derived from key segments, never stored folder objects (so the "folder-per-item" bug still can't recur). Env: `BLOB_READ_WRITE_TOKEN` (Florin provisions in Vercel). **This task ships the seam with NO behavior change yet тАФ provider exists, nothing calls it.**
- **FILES-1** Repoint **WRITE** paths to the seam: `api/drive/upload`, `TicketCaptureModal` (receipt capture), attachment hooks. Each upload calls `storage.put(...)` and **persists the returned `{key, url}` onto the owning record** (page property / attachment row) тАФ this is what kills "saved-but-not-findable": the file is found by its stored key on the record, never by walking a folder tree.
- **FILES-2** Repoint **READ/LIST/DELETE** paths: `FileManager*`, `DriveFileExplorer`, `DocumentManager`, `api/drive/list|route`. In-app explorer renders from `storage.list(prefix)` + record-stored keys. Delete via `storage.delete(key)`. **Explorer behavior by record type:** all record types render a FLAT file list per record (no manual folders тАФ keeps the no-mismanage guarantee). **Projects are the exception:** the project node renders its key subpaths as navigable virtual subfolders and supports create-folder / rename / move-within-project (a "folder" is created implicitly by uploading to/naming a new subpath тАФ no folder object is persisted). Move = re-key (copy to new key, update record ref, delete old). Subfolder UI is scoped to `recordType === 'project'` ONLY.
- **FILES-3** ЁЯй╕ **DATA MIGRATION (treat like SCHEMA-1b тАФ dry-run first, manifest, reversible).** Walk every tenant's existing Drive files, copy each into Blob under the new key scheme, update the owning record's stored URL/key. **Dry-run output:** per-tenant file count + total bytes + sample key mapping; Florin reviews before live. **Idempotent + resumable** (re-running skips already-copied keys). Keep Drive originals untouched until Florin verifies (Drive = the parachute; no snapshot needed since we don't delete source).
- **FILES-4** After Florin verifies files render in-app post-migration: retire dead Drive storage code (`api/drive/*` storage routes, `google-drive.ts` storage fns) тАФ **but keep Calendar/Gmail OAuth.** Leave Drive files in place as cold backup (don't delete remote).
- **FILES-5** Quotations engine тАФ **image insert must open the new in-app file explorer (picker mode), not a native dialog.** Current: `src/components/admin/quotations/FinancialRowRenderer.tsx:493` does `const url = prompt('Image URL:'); document.execCommand('insertImage', false, url)`. Replace the `prompt()` with the FILES explorer opened as a **picker**: user picks/uploads an image тЖТ explorer returns the file's served key/URL (via the FILES-ISO auth route) тЖТ insert that into the rich-text block. **Kill the native `prompt()` system window entirely.** Same native-dialog smell sits at `:496` (`prompt('Link URL:')`) тАФ out of scope for "image" but flag it: ideally both move to in-app UI, not browser prompts. (Depends on FILES-0/1/2 explorer existing.)
- **SCAN-4 depends on FILES-0/1** тАФ storing the original receipt file uses the same seam + key scheme.

## SCAN тАФ Receipts/expense capture (v0.4, free-tier core)
- **SCAN-5** ЁЯй╣тП░ **VAT-URGENT тАФ PDF capture broken for receipts & purchase invoices (Florin 2026-06-17, evidence + screenshot). THREE bugs, same modal (`TicketCaptureModal` is shared, `isInvoiceMode` flag):**
  1. **Receipts file input is IMAGE-ONLY.** `TicketCaptureModal` L501: `accept={isInvoiceMode ? 'image/*,application/pdf' : 'image/*'}` тЖТ receipts can't select a PDF. **FIX:** accept `image/*,application/pdf` in BOTH modes.
  2. **Server PDF parsing FAILS for ALL PDFs** (the "This PDF could not be opened. It may be corrupted." message). NOT the files тАФ `api/scan/route.ts` `getDocument()` (L78) throws on every PDF (тЖТ L86 `PDF_LOAD_ERROR` тЖТ L369 message). Cause: pdfjs serverless setup тАФ `GlobalWorkerOptions.workerSrc = ''` (L76) + the legacy ESM build inside a Vercel Node function fails to initialise. **FIX:** make PDF text-extraction work in serverless тАФ recommended: switch to a serverless-first extractor (**`unpdf`** / `pdfjs-serverless`) for the text layer; for scanned image-PDFs (no text) render page-1 for OCR via the same lib (canvas on Vercel is the second fragile point). MEASURE: log the real `getDocument` error first. This is the core bug behind BOTH "can't process PDF" reports.
  3. **Manual entry with NO document = illegal for VAT (Florin).** The "enter manually" path saves fields without the source file. **FIX:** manual entry MUST allow attaching the original photo/PDF, stored on the record like a scanned one (ties to SCAN-4 / FILES store-the-original). A receipt/invoice record without its document is not acceptable.
  **VERIFY (as a tenant, before VAT season):** upload a PDF receipt AND a PDF purchase invoice тЖТ both scan/parse with no "corrupted" error; manual entry lets you attach + stores the file; the record shows the document. (Pairs with SCAN-1 = the saved record actually lands in the tenant's grid.)
- **SCAN-1** ЁЯй╣ тП░ **VAT-URGENT (Florin: trimester VAT declaration next month тАФ manual receipt/invoice entry MUST work).** Manually adding a ticket from the scan modal produces NO result in the DB. ROOT-CAUSE HYPOTHESIS (Planner, measured): `TicketCaptureModal.handleSave` creates the page with HARDCODED bare ids тАФ `createPageServerFirst('db-expenses', тАж)` (L261) / `createPageServerFirst('db-tickets', тАж)` (L274) тАФ instead of the tenant-resolved id (`targetDatabaseId` is already a prop; use it / `resolveDbId`). On multi-tenant the real DB is `db-tickets-{suffix}` тЖТ the record lands on a non-matching base id and never shows in the tenant's grid. (SCHEMA-1a's server-side resolution MAY mask this тАФ UNVERIFIED.) **FIX:** use the resolved `targetDatabaseId` in `handleSave`, not the hardcoded name. **VERIFY:** as a tenant, add a receipt AND a purchase invoice manually тЖТ both appear in their grids. **Florin: TEST this on the live app first тАФ it may already work via SCHEMA-1a; if not, this fix.**
- **SCAN-2** ЁЯй╣ **Can't upload PDF receipts on desktop тАФ ROOT CAUSE FOUND (Planner 2026-06-09): client-side Tesseract OCR gate chokes on PDFs (FREE tier).** `TicketCaptureModal.tsx` `runScan` (L133-156): on FREE tier it runs `recognizeReceipt` (client Tesseract, `@/lib/ocr`) on the file BEFORE the server call тАФ but **Tesseract reads images only, not PDFs** тЖТ a PDF throws (L151) тЖТ catch sets error + **`return` (L154), so `/api/scan` is NEVER called** тАФ even though the server route HANDLES PDFs (pdfjs text-extract + first-page render fallback, `api/scan/route.ts` L63-126). Images work; Pro works (skips client OCR). **FIX (two changes in `runScan`):** (1) **Gate client OCR to images only:** `if (isFree && file.type.startsWith('image/'))` тАФ PDFs/non-images bypass Tesseract and go straight to `/api/scan` (server handles them). (2) **On client-OCR failure, fall THROUGH to the server scan** instead of `return` (don't let a Tesseract hiccup abort the upload тАФ server is the fallback). **VERIFY:** as a FREE tenant on desktop, upload a PDF receipt тЖТ it scans via the server (pdfjs), pre-fills the form, no Acrobat hand-off / dead modal; image upload still works.
- **SCAN-3** Receipts: remove details view (GRID-6); in the modal тАФ remove journal entry, ADD project-connection property, and replace the journal section with an **image/file component** that displays the receipt (img/pdf/etc.). (was B2 + Florin financials)
- **SCAN-4** Store the ORIGINAL receipt file (not just extracted data) тАФ see SCAN-3 display depends on it. (was B2 core)

## SEND тАФ Send invoice/quote (v0.4, happy-path)
- **SEND-1** ЁЯй╣ "Send to client" says no email though email exists тАФ resolve email column by TYPE not name (locale-fragile). (was B5)
- **SEND-4** ЁЯй╣ **No tenant notification when a client signs a quote online тАФ follow-up loop incomplete (Florin 2026-06-09).** MEASURED: the signature flow EXISTS and works тАФ public viewer `/quote/[id]` captures draw/type/upload signature тЖТ `accept-quote.ts` sets `status:"ACCEPTED"` + `clientSignature/signatureMethod/consentName/signedAt` + auto-creates the project (`autoCreateProjectFromQuote`). BUT `acceptQuotation` sends **NO email** тАФ tenant is never told their quote was signed. **FIX:** in `accept-quote.ts`, after the status update, send a Resend notification to **`tenant.email`** ("Quote {title} accepted & signed by {consentName} on {date}", link to the quote/new project). Source tenant email via `quote.database.tenantId` тЖТ tenant record (already fetched at L44-47 for the project step). Skip gracefully if no email. Optionally also send the client a confirmation copy. **ALSO (verify, likely bug):** the viewer writes the RAW string `status:"ACCEPTED"` but the system uses canonical option IDs elsewhere (code checks BOTH `'ACCEPTED'` and `'opt-accepted'`, L25) тЖТ the admin quotation grid may not show the quote as Accepted (status-ID-vs-string mismatch, SCHEMA-2 class). Write the canonical `opt-accepted` (or map on read) so the signed quote displays correctly. **VERIFY:** sign a quote as the client тЖТ tenant gets the email; the quote shows Accepted in the admin grid; the project was created.
- **SEND-3** ЁЯй╣ **No self-copy + no reply-to on sent quotes/invoices (Florin 2026-06-08).** MEASURED: `send-quote.ts` + `send-invoice.ts` set only `from: "${company} <noreply@coral-group.be>"` + `to: [clientEmail]` тАФ NO `cc`, NO `bcc`, NO `replyTo`. So the tenant keeps no copy/record of what they sent, and a client hitting Reply lands on Coral's no-reply void (replies lost). Multi-tenant impact: every tenant sends from Coral's noreply with no path back to them. **FIX (both actions):** (1) add **`bcc: [tenant.email]`** (BCC not CC тАФ client must not see the internal address) so the tenant gets a copy/delivery confirmation; (2) add **`replyTo: tenant.email`** so client replies reach the actual business. Source `tenant.email` from the profile (pass it into the action, same place `companyName` is already passed). Skip BCC/replyTo gracefully if `tenant.email` is empty. **VERIFY:** send a quote тЖТ tenant receives a BCC copy; reply to the received client email тЖТ goes to tenant.email, not noreply.
- **SEND-2** ЁЯй╣ **Credit notes sent over Peppol as INVOICES, not credit notes тЖТ `PEPPOL_INTERNAL_ERROR`.** Planner-VALIDATED coder plan (OK to proceed). ROOT CAUSES (both confirmed in code): (1) `ClientInvoiceEngine.tsx` `handleSendPeppol` (~L753 body) OMITS `isCreditNote` + `parentInvoiceId` тЖТ backend defaults `undefined` тЖТ builds doc as INVOICE. **Backend is ALREADY correct** (`api/peppol/send/route.ts`: L171 `document_type: isCreditNote?'CREDIT_NOTE':'INVOICE'`, L261 UBL `type: isCreditNote?'381':'380'`, L153 parent ref) тАФ it just never gets the flag. FIX = pass the two fields in the body. (2) L332 reads `validateData` (`.json()`) BEFORE the `.ok` check тЖТ non-JSON error page throws тЖТ generic `PEPPOL_INTERNAL_ERROR`; guard the 3 `.json()` calls with try/catchтЖТ`.text()` fallback. **EVIDENCE:** Coral outbox (peppol debug 2026-06-07) shows every `CN-2026-xxx` as `document_type:"INVOICE"` тАФ proves the bug. **тЪая╕П REAL-WORLD IMPACT:** the ~6 credit notes already sent to Reno-K went out AS INVOICES тАФ recipient may book them as PAYABLES not credits тЖТ re-issue as proper credit notes after fix + confirm with Reno-K. **PLANNER ADDITIONS to coder plan:** (a) verify the UBL BillingReference uses the parent invoice NUMBER (e.g. "2026-19"), not the internal doc id; (b) verification must SEND a CN and confirm via `/api/peppol/inbox?debug=1` that outbox now shows `document_type: CREDIT_NOTE` (not just that the flag propagates).

## NOTIF тАФ In-app notifications: persistent toast + bell menu (NEW, v0.4 toast / v0.5 bell)
**Scope:** invoice + quote events first. **SERVER-PERSISTED** (state survives reload + cross-device тАФ a toast must reappear until the user actually checks the item). Toasts via the EXISTING `sonner` `<Toaster>` (already mounted `AdminLayout.tsx` L565, top-right). Bell lives in the `AdminLayout` header (L385 region). NO notification model/API exists yet тАФ build foundation first. Coder: follow exactly; one NOTIF-x = one commit; `/pd` measure + tsc/lint green each step.

- **NOTIF-0 тАФ PREREQUISITE (verify/patch first).** Confirm `session.user.id` is populated. `auth.ts` session callback (L218-224) sets role/tenantId/etc. but NOT `id` тАФ add `(session.user as any).id = token.sub` (or equivalent) so the API's user-guard + mark-read scoping work. Without this, NOTIF user-scoping is broken. (For v1 we emit tenant-wide `userId=null`, but the read-guard still needs `session.user.id`.)
- **NOTIF-1 тАФ Data model + API (foundation, build first).**
  - Prisma `Notification` model: `id String @id @default(cuid())`, `tenantId String` (FKтЖТTenant, **@index**), `userId String?` (target user; `null` = all users of the tenant / owner), `type String` (one of: `QUOTE_ACCEPTED`,`QUOTE_VIEWED`,`INVOICE_PAID`,`INVOICE_OVERDUE`,`INVOICE_SENT`,`CREDIT_NOTE`,`PEPPOL_RECEIVED`), `title String`, `body String`, `entityType String` (`quote`|`invoice`|`project`), `entityId String` (**@index** тАФ the GlobalPage/record id the notif concerns), `href String` (deep link, e.g. `/admin/financials/income/invoices/{id}`), `readAt DateTime?`, `createdAt DateTime @default(now())`. Composite index `@@index([tenantId, userId, readAt, createdAt])`. Migration required.
  - Central helper `src/lib/notifications.ts` тЖТ `createNotification({tenantId, userId?, type, title, body, entityType, entityId, href})`. SINGLE insertion point тАФ every emitter calls only this (never `prisma.notification.create` inline).
  - API (all session-guarded, tenant-scoped, NEVER cross-tenant; match `tenantId` AND (`userId === session.user.id` OR `userId === null`)):
    - `GET /api/notifications?status=unread|all&cursor=` тЖТ `{ items, unreadCount, nextCursor }`, newest-first, page size 20.
    - `POST /api/notifications/mark-read` body `{ ids?: string[], entityId?: string, all?: boolean }` тЖТ sets `readAt=now()`. **`entityId` form is the "checked the concerned item" trigger** (marks ALL notifs for that item read). All three forms supported.
  - Acceptance: createтЖТlistтЖТmark-read round-trips; cross-tenant request returns nothing.

- **NOTIF-2 тАФ Event emitters (invoice + quote).** Emit `userId=null` (tenant-wide тАФ all tenant users see it; DO NOT resolve owner now). Call `createNotification` at each REAL state change (not on every save). **There is NO single invoice-status chokepoint тАФ emit at BOTH transition sites (don't miss the manual one):**
  - `accept-quote.ts` after status update тЖТ `QUOTE_ACCEPTED`, `href`=quote (in-app twin of SEND-4's email; both fire here).
  - **Auto** status path `src/app/actions/pages.ts` (~L326 sets `newStatus='opt-paid'` from payment matching) тЖТ `INVOICE_PAID`.
  - **Manual** status path = the engine status-select (FIN-5, `ClientInvoiceEngine`) / its server write тЖТ `INVOICE_PAID`/`INVOICE_SENT`/`INVOICE_OVERDUE` as set; CN creation (`handleCreateCreditNote`) тЖТ `CREDIT_NOTE`.
  - `lib/dunning.ts` тЖТ `INVOICE_OVERDUE` when an invoice crosses due.
  - **STRONGLY PREFERRED:** centralize invoice-status writes into ONE helper and emit there, so both auto+manual paths share a single emit site. If not centralizing, emit at every site above тАФ missing the manual path is a fail.
  - **Idempotency MANDATORY:** never emit twice for the same `(entityId, type)` тАФ guard by comparing previous vs new status before emitting (no notif if status didn't actually change).

- **NOTIF-3 тАФ Persistent toast: on app-open AND on status-change (the core behavior Florin specified).** Add a client component `NotificationWatcher` mounted once in `AdminLayout`.
  - **On app open (mount):** `GET /api/notifications?status=unread`. For EACH unread, fire a `sonner` toast with **`duration: Infinity`** (must NOT auto-dismiss), **`id: notification.id`** (dedupe тАФ re-mounts/HMR must not stack duplicates), and an action button **"View"** тЖТ navigates to `href`, calls `mark-read {ids:[id]}`, dismisses. The toast's **close (├Ч) dismisses WITHOUT marking read** (so it reappears next app-open until the item is genuinely checked).
  - **On status-change while app is open:** the watcher POLLS `GET /api/notifications?status=unread` every **30s** AND on window `focus`; any unread id not already shown this session fires the same persistent toast. (Polling now; SSE/Realtime = noted future upgrade, do NOT build now.)
  - **"Persists until the user checks the concerned item" тАФ exact semantics:** a notif clears ONLY when its `entityId` is opened. Implement by having each invoice/quote detail page call `POST /api/notifications/mark-read {entityId}` on mount тЖТ server unread drops тЖТ toast won't refire on next open + bell badge decrements. Clicking "View" also clears. Dismissing the toast does NOT clear. Reloading the app with the item still unchecked тЖТ toast fires again.
  - Acceptance: trigger a status change тЖТ toast appears and stays; reload тЖТ still there; open the item тЖТ gone permanently.

- **NOTIF-4 тАФ Bell menu + history (development plan; build AFTER NOTIF-1..3 verified).**
  - Bell icon button in the `AdminLayout` header (L385 region) with an **unread-count badge** (from `unreadCount`); 0 тЖТ no badge.
  - Dropdown panel: full notification HISTORY (read + unread), newest-first, infinite-scroll/paginated via `cursor` (`status=all`). Unread visually distinct (dot + subtle bg). Each row: type icon, title, body, relative time; click тЖТ navigate to `href` + mark that one read. Panel header action: **"Mark all read"** (`mark-read {all:true}`). History is NOT auto-deleted тАФ user consults at own discretion (retention policy = later).
  - Mobile: surface the bell/badge in the mobile shell (`MobileShell`) too.
  - Acceptance: bell badge matches unread count; opening history + mark-all-read zeroes the badge; clicking a row deep-links correctly.
  - **Cross-refs:** SEND-4 (email channel for QUOTE_ACCEPTED тАФ NOTIF is the in-app channel, same trigger), `lib/dunning.ts` (overdue), FIN status changes, PROFILE (owner/user scoping).

## PEPPOL тАФ Receive (v0.4, happy-path; partly provider-side)
- **PEPPOL-2** тЬЕ RESOLVED 2026-06-04 (e-invoice.be support reply): Coral = approved RESELLER. Credits at ORG level, post-pay NET-10, **no per-tenant activation/fee, no per-tenant credit pack**. Reseller-created tenants are billed via the org account тЖТ **NOT subject to the pre-paid "blocked until payment" gate тЖТ they can RECEIVE from go-live.** 1 credit per Peppol doc BOTH directions; tiered тВм0.18тЖТтВм0.05 by total monthly volume across all tenants. Per-tenant balance via `GET https://api.e-invoice.be/api/stats`. (was E1 тАФ closed.)
- **PEPPOL-1** ЁЯЯвтЖТ provider-handled: the `smp_registration: false` gate was the regular pre-paid model, which does NOT apply to reseller tenants. e-invoice.be is re-triggering Coral's SMP server-side. **Florin action:** confirm to support that Coral is the tenant to push first (done on ticket). **Verify:** once they confirm, (a) Coral shows `smp_registration: true`, (b) a real inbound doc lands in Coral's inbox, (c) a freshly reseller-provisioned test tenant comes up receive-enabled with NO gate. - **PEPPOL-3** ЁЯй╣ **Inbound docs not reaching ERP тАФ ACCOUNT-SPLIT ROUTING (not a code bug).** Two separate e-invoice identities for the same company: (1) ORIGINAL direct account (self-signup) where Peppol ID `0208:1018865828` is SMP-registered / where inbound lands; (2) RESELLER tenant (`cmneyas2b0000veqvkgl2luz1`, key `api-454sтАжqj8b`) that the ERP reads. NOT linked тЖТ inbound (incl. yesterday's test invoice) lands in the original; ERP polls reseller inbox тЖТ empty. **CODE CORRECT.** тЬЕ CONFIRMED via `/api/peppol/inbox?debug=1` (2026-06-07): inbox/invoices/creditNotes all `total:0`, `raw_outbox total:7` (sending works, key valid) тЖТ inbound not routed to reseller tenant. **тЪая╕П DO NOT authorize support's "delete original account" until Peppol ID is re-registered to the RESELLER tenant** тАФ deleting while original holds the SMP reg = inbound BOUNCES. **SAFE SEQUENCE:** support migrates/registers `0208:1018865828` to reseller tenant (smp_registration:true) тЖТ send test тЖТ verify in ERP тЖТ THEN delete original. Attach the debug output (empty inbox + 7-doc outbox) as evidence. [re-added after concurrent-write clobber 2026-06-07]
  - **IDENTIFIERS (confirmed live via `/api/peppol/onboard` 2026-06-08):** `eInvoiceTenantId: ten-gar163w6fd093s8w` ┬╖ `peppolId: 0208:1018865828` (VAT BE1018865828) ┬╖ company "BV CORAL ENTERPRISES". (NOT our Prisma id `cmneyas2b0000veqvkgl2luz1` тАФ useless to e-invoice.)
  - **тЬЕ PROVIDER ACTED тАФ CORRECT STEPS (e-invoice reply 2026-06-12, Planner-verified vs expected sequence):** (1) production tenant `ten-gar163w6fd093s8w` (= the ERP's `eInvoiceTenantId`) now RECEIVES for `0208:1018865828`; (2) they REMOVED `0208:1018865828` from the original direct account ("your company in the management app" тАФ the stale one) тЖТ duplicate/conflicting registration cleared; (3) a test tenant `ten-dh674tl9adf4dz5j` is also configured for the ID but test tenants can't receive (FYI, harmless). This is exactly the migrate-to-reseller-then-remove-original sequence we specified. **REMAINING = Florin verify with a REAL inbound send тЖТ `/api/peppol/inbox?debug=1` inbox `total > 0` тЖТ then тЬЕ.** Then optionally delete the now-de-registered original account. If inbound STILL fails, re-check the prod-vs-test dual-config.
  - **REFINED DIAGNOSIS (2026-06-08): DUPLICATE/CONFLICTING REGISTRATION, not a simple split.** `/api/peppol/onboard` shows the RESELLER tenant ALREADY `peppolRegistered: true`, `peppolStatus: "ACTIVE (External SMP)"`. So reseller IS registered+active, yet inbox empty тЖТ the Peppol ID is likely registered on TWO SMPs (stale original account's AP + reseller's external SMP) and the network root pointer (SML) for `0208:1018865828` still resolves to the ORIGINAL account's access point тЖТ inbound routes there. **Cleanup must fix ROUTING, not just delete a row:** ensure SML/SMP for `0208:1018865828` points to the AP serving `ten-gar163w6fd093s8w`, remove the conflicting original registration, test delivery before/after. **Florin is transmitting this to e-invoice support 2026-06-08.** Safe order unchanged: confirm reseller owns the SML pointer тЖТ test inbound lands in ERP тЖТ THEN delete original.
- **PEPPOL-4** ЁЯФ┤ **REOPENED тАФ committed (PEPPOL-4 on main) but BROKEN IN PRACTICE (Florin 2026-06-17: 2 new invoices show "untitled" supplier, no original doc, sparse data). Deployment ruled out (main=develop). TWO confirmed root causes:**
  - **(A) Supplier "untitled" = WRONG STORE.** The purchase-invoice supplier relation targets the **`db-suppliers` GlobalDatabase** (`relationDatabaseId: 'db-suppliers'`), but `peppol/inbox/route.ts` auto-create does `prisma.supplier.create(...)` тЖТ a row in the **`Supplier` Prisma TABLE** тЖТ links the invoice to a Supplier-table id the relation CAN'T resolve тЖТ "untitled." Same mismatch on the VAT pre-match (`prisma.supplier.findMany`). **FIX:** match + auto-create the supplier as a **`db-suppliers` GlobalPage** (resolve via `getLockedDbId('db-suppliers')` + `createPage`, set name/VAT/address as its properties), and link the invoice relation to THAT page id. Stop using the `Supplier` table for this relation.
  - **(B) Original document silently skipped.** PDF fetch is gated `if (tenant.driveFolderId && process.env.GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID)` (L282) тЖТ if the tenant has no `driveFolderId` (or env missing), no original is stored, no error. **FIX:** don't silently skip тАФ store the fetched PDF regardless (Blob once FILES lands; until then ensure Drive folder exists or log loudly). Drive dependency is the fragility FILES-Blob removes.
  - **(C) "sparse data" тАФ VERIFY:** look at an actual record (`/api/peppol/inbox?debug=1` or DB) to see if totals/lines are empty because the e-invoice `DocumentResponse` for those docs is sparse (parse issue) vs the mapping. Don't assume.
  - **This means PEPPOL-4's earlier "complete" was code-present, not working. Re-verify on a REAL inbound from a new supplier: supplier resolves to a named db-suppliers page; original doc stored+viewable; totals/lines populated.**
  -- (original gap list, still valid for the rewrite below) --
  **Inbound invoices now arrive тЬЕ but the record MAPPING is incomplete (Florin 2026-06-15).** MEASURED in `api/peppol/inbox/route.ts` `globalPage.create` (L264-289): three gaps + a view gap.
  1. **Supplier relation empty for new suppliers.** `supplier: [matchedSupplierId]` is filled ONLY if `matchSupplier(vendorVat)` finds an EXISTING supplier contact by VAT (L187). New supplier тЖТ no match тЖТ empty relation (the `supplierName`/`supplierVat` TEXT is set, but nothing is linked). **FIX:** when no VAT match, **auto-create the supplier contact** from `vendor_name`/`vendor_tax_id`/`vendor_address` and link it (so the relation fills). Idempotent on VAT (don't create dupes тАФ ties to FIN-10 identity rule).
  2. **No original document stored.** Record keeps only `peppolDocId` + parsed fields; `blocks: []`, no attachment тЖТ "I don't have the document." **FIX:** fetch the source document via `getInboxDocument(apiKey, doc.id)` (already in `e-invoice-inbox.ts`) and STORE it on the record (PDF/UBL), viewable in the detail view. Ties to **FILES (Blob)** + SCAN-4 (store-the-original).
  3. **Line items dumped, not structured.** Lines stored as `invoiceLines: JSON.stringify(...)` (a string property) + first line's text shoved into `betreft` (the subject) тЖТ "items go in the description." **FIX:** write the parsed `lines` as **structured line-item blocks** (the same `Block[]` the expense/invoice engine renders) so they show as proper rows; stop putting line text in `betreft`.
  4. **VIEW: extend GRID-10 to `db-expenses`.** Inbound invoices open in the generic `PageModal` (same fragmentation as projects) тЖТ make the type-aware modal route purchase-invoice/expense records to the proper `PurchaseInvoiceEngine` view, not the generic property dump. (Florin's hope is correct тАФ GRID-10 is part of this, but it must cover `db-expenses` too.)
  5. **PDF/download must serve the ORIGINAL document, not a regenerated stub.** CONFIRMED via Florin's download (`purchase-invoice-2218404561.pdf`, 2026-06-15): the modal's "PDF" button generated a CoralOS doc with `FROM (SUPPLIER): тАФ` (empty), `No line item detail available`, buyer=Coral тАФ i.e. a sparse regenerated stub, "not a valid financial document." The download/view must serve the **stored source document** (UBL-rendered / the supplier's actual PDF from gap #2), never a regenerated stub.
  **VERIFY:** receive a Peppol invoice from a NEW supplier тЖТ supplier contact auto-created + linked (FROM no longer empty); the ORIGINAL document is attached + rendered (right pane) + downloadable as the source; line items render as structured ORDERLIJNEN rows (not a JSON blob / betreft / "no line item detail"); the record opens in the split-pane purchase view (GRID-10), not the generic modal.
- **PEPPOL-5** ЁЯй╕ **BACKFILL тАФ re-hydrate ALREADY-received inbound invoices (Florin 2026-06-17).** Invoices received BEFORE the AGG-2 mapping fix are missing supplier link / original document / structured line blocks. The data is STILL re-fetchable: each record carries `peppolDocId`, and the tenant's `eInvoiceApiKey` + `getInboxDocument`/`getInboxDocumentPdf` re-pull the source тАФ no need for the senders to resend. **Operation (treat like SCHEMA-1b тАФ dry-run тЖТ Florin-approve тЖТ execute, idempotent):**
  - Scope: existing `db-expenses` records with `source: 'src-peppol'` (or `peppolDocId` present) that are MISSING data (empty `supplier` relation OR no `receiptUrl` OR empty `blocks`). Per tenant, using that tenant's key.
  - For each: re-fetch by `peppolDocId` тЖТ re-run the AGG-2 mapping in UPDATE mode: (a) match/auto-create + link supplier; (b) fetch the original PDF тЖТ store тЖТ set `receiptUrl`; (c) rebuild structured `financial-row` blocks from the lines.
  - **Idempotent + non-destructive:** fill only EMPTY fields тАФ NEVER overwrite user edits (manual supplier/category/notes). Skip records already complete. Re-runnable.
  - **No double credit-count:** do NOT call `incrementPeppolReceived` (these were already counted); re-fetching a received doc must not consume a new credit тАФ VERIFY with e-invoice that `getInboxDocument` on an already-received doc is free.
  - Delivery: an admin/superadmin script or a guarded API route (not auto). **Dry-run output:** per-tenant count of records to backfill + sample. **VERIFY:** after run, previously-received invoices show supplier + original document + ORDERLIJNEN; no credits consumed; user-edited fields untouched. (SUPERVISED тАФ data op.)

## INBOX тАФ Email (v0.5)
- **INBOX-1** ЁЯй╣ Inbox doesn't download mail though accounts are connected. **ROOT CAUSE FOUND (Planner 2026-06): OAuth scope mismatch.** The connect flow (`api/email/connect/google/route.ts`) requests Gmail **API** scopes тАФ `gmail.readonly`, `gmail.modify`, `gmail.send`, `userinfo.*` тАФ but the sync engine (`api/email/route.ts`) connects over **IMAP via XOAUTH2** (`imapflow`). Gmail IMAP requires the **`https://mail.google.com/`** scope, which is NOT requested. So OAuth succeeds + the account is stored + redirect says `connected=true` ("seemingly connected"), but every `client.connect()` is rejected for missing scope тЖТ 500 "Failed to sync with IMAP provider." **TWO FIXES тАФ Florin decides (this is a launch-relevant fork):**
  - **(A) Switch Gmail sync to the Gmail REST API** (recommended). Use `googleapis` gmail.users.messages.list/get instead of imapflow for Gmail accounts тАФ aligns with the scopes ALREADY granted, no restricted-scope verification. `gmail.readonly` is "sensitive" (lighter Google review) vs `mail.google.com` which is "restricted" (full CASA security audit, slow/costly). Keeps imapflow only for true generic-IMAP providers.
  - **(B) Add `https://mail.google.com/` to the connect scopes** (quick, keeps imapflow). BUT it's a RESTRICTED scope тЖТ Google requires a security assessment before production; until verified you're capped at 100 users + "unverified app" screen. Fine for your own/test accounts, a launch blocker at scale.
  тЖТ **Recommendation: (A)** for Gmail to dodge restricted-scope verification; design a provider adapter (Gmail API / Graph / generic-IMAP) so INBOX-2 multi-account is clean. **MEASURE first:** add the real IMAP error to the response/log to confirm the auth-scope rejection before changing.
  - Secondary (note, not the bug): OAuth `state` is the raw tenantId (no CSRF token); `connectedEmailAccount` upsert is keyed by `email` GLOBALLY, not per-tenant (two tenants, same address = collision). Tidy when touching this.
- **INBOX-2** All-inboxes unified view.
- **INBOX-3** Link a mail to sales/quote/project; a mail linked to a sales-pipeline item propagates to the connected quotation and onward to the project (cascade linking).

Outlook + Apple are NOT built. **To add them, fundamental first:** make the event model provider-agnostic тАФ rename/add `provider` + `externalEventId` + `externalCalendarId` (migrate existing `googleEventId`тЖТ`externalEventId` w/ `provider='google'`), then add adapters: **Outlook = Microsoft Graph** (`/me/events`, MSAL OAuth) ; **Apple = CalDAV** (app-specific password; no OAuth) . Don't bolt provider #2 onto Google-named columns тАФ that's the recurring "identity vs name" trap at the schema level. Settings UI then lists connected accounts per provider (mirror the email account-connect pattern).

Build a dedicated `m/calendar` view (agenda/day list, thumb-reachable add, no desktop grid).

## BANK тАФ Bank connection / transaction feed (v0.5 feature; research done)
- **BANK-1** ЁЯУК **RESEARCH (Planner 2026-06).** GOAL: pull bank transactions (AIS) into `db-payments-in`, then **auto-match paymentтЖТinvoice by structured communication / OGM** (matching mechanism already designed in history). Read (AIS) first; payment initiation (PIS, pay suppliers) much later.
  - **KEY FEASIBILITY WIN:** use a LICENSED aggregator тЖТ THEY are the regulated AISP, so **CoralOS does NOT need its own PSD2/AISP licence.** That removes the biggest barrier.
  - **RECOMMENDED: Ponto (Isabel Group / Ibanity)** тАФ Belgian-native (Isabel = the country's banking-rails incumbent), 1,800+ EU banks, **specializes in BUSINESS/corporate accounts** (most aggregators are retail-first тАФ decisive for a B2B construction SaaS), AIS + PIS, **Partner-Paying pricing** (bill into your SaaS margin, volume-based, not public тАФ get a quote), free sandbox + good docs/Slack. Best strategic + geographic fit.
  - **ALTERNATIVE (MVP/cost): GoCardless Bank Account Data** (ex-Nordigen) тАФ free AIS tier, 2,200+ EU banks, fast to prototype; more retail-oriented, rate-limited free tier. Good for a cheap proof-of-concept.
  - **ADJACENT (accountant flow, not live API): CodaBox** тАФ Belgian CODA/SODA delivery via fiduciaries; fits the accountant-export side, not real-time feed. Note for later.
  - **PSD2 constraints to design for (all aggregators):** 90-day SCA re-consent тЖТ build a reconnect/renew-consent UX (don't assume a connection lasts forever); per-tenant connection + token storage (same adapter pattern as email/calendar); read-only scope first.
  - **ARCHITECTURE:** provider adapter тЖТ normalize transactions тЖТ upsert into `db-payments-in` (idempotent on bank txn id) тЖТ OGM/structured-comm exact-match to invoice (identity match, NOT substring тАФ recurring rule). Reuse the FILES-ISO-style per-tenant isolation.
  - **VERDICT:** feasible, clean via aggregator, but it's a **v0.5 feature with onboarding lead time** (sandbox immediately; production needs business verification with Ponto). RECOMMEND: open a Ponto sandbox to prototype the AISтЖТOGM-match loop in parallel while the free-tier launch proceeds тАФ don't block launch on it. **Florin decision needed:** Ponto (strategic, paid) vs GoCardless (cheap MVP) for the first spike.
- **BANK-2** ЁЯУК **PONTO DEEP-DIVE тАФ implementation + costs (Planner 2026-06).**
  - **AUTH/INTEGRATION (Ibanity Ponto Connect):** OAuth2 **authorization-code + PKCE** for the user's initial bank-account link тЖТ then **refresh-token flow**. Access token = 30 min; refresh token valid 90 days but **refreshable indefinitely** (refresh before expiry тЖТ connection persists; if a tenant goes >90 days idle, re-consent). Scopes: **`ai`** (account info) or **`ai pi`** (+ payment initiation later). Per-tenant token storage (same adapter pattern as email/calendar).
  - **тЪая╕П IMPLEMENTATION GOTCHA (matters for our Vercel/Node stack):** Ibanity requires **mutual TLS (client certificate)** on EVERY server-to-server call. In Node = an `https.Agent({cert,key,ca})` (or undici dispatcher) built from a cert Ibanity issues you. On Vercel serverless: store cert+key as base64 env vars, build the agent per request (cold-start cost). Ibanity provides the application/eIDAS-level certs themselves (they're the licensed AISP) тАФ so we do NOT chase PSD2 QWAC/QSEAL certs ourselves. SDKs exist (.NET confirmed; Node/others available) тАФ or call REST directly with the mTLS agent. Sandbox + webhooks (transaction notifications) + open Slack support, all free.
  - **GO-LIVE:** sandbox is immediate + free; production = a "Go Live" verification with Ibanity/Ponto (business onboarding) тАФ the lead-time item.
  - **COSTS:** integration is FREE; you pay only usage. **AIS тЙИ тВм4/month per linked bank account**, **tiered down as account count grows**. PIS (payment initiation) billed **per executed payment** (later). Two billing models: **Partner-paying** (Ponto bills CoralOS, tiered; we mark it up / fold into a plan тАФ more invoicing work) or **Customer-paying** (Ponto bills the tenant directly тАФ ZERO invoicing work for us, cleanest for a SaaS). Ponto = payment institution licensed by the National Bank of Belgium.
  - **PRICING-FIT TAKE:** at ~тВм4/acct/mo, bank-feed is a natural **paid-tier feature** (one account per self-employed tenant тЙИ тВм4 cost тЖТ price it inside a PRO add-on, or use Customer-paying so it never hits our P&L). Get a partner quote for the tiered rate before committing. [refs: myponto.com/en/pricing/partner-paying-model, documentation.ibanity.com/ponto-connect]

## TT тАФ Time-Tracker CONSOLIDATION (ЁЯФТ SUPERVISED тАФ Florin 2026-06-17: do this FIRST, before mobile)
**MEASURED (Planner): the time-tracker is a half-migrated PARALLEL APP embedded in CoralOS, not a native module.** It carries its own duplicate `components/ui/*` (full shadcn set), own `i18n/` + `locales`, own `contexts/` (ThemeContext + a Supabase `AuthContext`), own `pages/`, and an `integrations/supabase` data layer. **SPLIT-BRAIN DATA:** part of it reads/writes **Supabase** (a SECOND database тАФ announcements, documents, TimesheetView, LateEntry, ApprovalManager, UserDetailView, auth) while other hooks (`useClockEntries`, `useApprovalRequests`, `useScheduleAttachments`) use the app's Prisma/Neon API. Consolidation = fully absorb it onto CoralOS's stack and retire the parallel infra. **Phased, each phase its own commit; Florin-gated.**
- **TT-0 тАФ AUDIT (Planner-led, partly done).** Exhaustive map: every Supabase read/write (table тЖТ feature), every duplicate `ui/` component vs the app's, the parallel i18n/theme/auth, and тАФ CRITICAL тАФ whether the Supabase data is **tenant-scoped** (if TT data has no `tenantId` isolation, it's a cross-tenant data-leak risk; treat as launch-blocking before TT ships to tenants). Output = migration map + isolation verdict.
- **TT-1 тАФ DATA off Supabase тЖТ Prisma/Neon (the core).** Per feature (announcements, documents, timesheets, late entries, approvals, user detail), move storage to the app's Prisma schema + API routes; ensure tenant scoping. Then delete `integrations/supabase`. Kills the second database + the data fragmentation. Highest value, do per-feature.
- **TT-2 тАФ AUTH.** Replace the Supabase `AuthContext` with the app's NextAuth session/tenant. One auth, tenant-scoped.
- **TT-3 тАФ UI.** Replace `time-tracker/components/ui/*` with the app's shared components; delete the duplicate set.
- **TT-4 тАФ i18n + THEME.** Fold its `i18n/locales` into next-intl (NL/FR/EN/RO) and its ThemeContext into the app theme.
- **TT-5 тАФ Make it a tenant-scoped MODULE** behaving like the rest (gating via `PLAN_MODULES`, lockedDbIds where relevant). **VERIFY:** time-tracker runs entirely on CoralOS auth/data/UI; no Supabase; data tenant-isolated; HR timesheets/schedule/leave all work.

## MOBILE тАФ App-wide mobile-friendliness (ЁЯФТ SUPERVISED тАФ Florin: AFTER time-tracker consolidation, v0.4)
**MEASURED: mobile coverage is PARTIAL + inconsistent.** `/m` has only `clients, settings, purchases, invoices, quotes, expenses` тАФ MISSING dashboard, projects, tasks, calendar, contacts, suppliers, library, inbox, files, time-tracker. So most modules fall back to desktop layouts on phone ("topsy turvy"). **FIRST DECISION (Florin's call тАФ I'll recommend): strategy.** (A) keep building per-module `/m` routes (current path тАФ duplicated UI, drifts) OR (B) **make the main app responsive** (one codebase, responsive layouts + a mobile shell/nav) тАФ fewer surfaces, no drift, the modern default. **Recommend B**, with `/m` kept only where a genuinely different mobile flow is needed (capture/scan). Then a per-module pass.
**тЪая╕П PROTECT THE EXISTING `/m/` FREE-TIER SURFACE (Florin 2026-06-19, binding).** `/m/*` (own `MobileShell`, reuses the shared engines тЖТ already inherits FIN-NUM/INV-DUEDATE/SELECT-UNIFY/INV-PDF-POLISH) is in DECENT shape. DO NOT regress it. Any change to a SHARED component must be mobile-first (add width, never break `/m/`). After ANY MOBILE work, VERIFY the `/m/` pages (invoices, quotes, clients, expenses, purchases, settings) still look + work.
- **MOB-1** ЁЯЯб PARTIAL (coder `8d5d31c`: manifest-mobile scope `/m` + a weak client-side AdminLayout redirect). **STILL the waitlisted problem (Florin 2026-06-20: "mobile routing still has the same problem").** See MOB-ROUTE for the real fix.
- **ЁЯЯа MOB-ROUTE тАФ FREE mobile lands in the wrong place (desktop/WORKHUB) instead of `/m`. The proper server-side fix for the long-waitlisted routing bug. тЪая╕П RE-VERIFY NEEDED: Florin's "still broken" report (2026-06-20) was from the CORAL account (FOUNDER/paid) тАФ the redirect is `if (planType!=='FREE') return`, so paid tiers are intentionally NOT redirected; that symptom was expected. Florin is now re-testing on a FREE account. The server-side fix below is still valid for the GENUINE gaps regardless of that re-test (workhub branch has no redirect; PWA installed from desktop has start_url:/admin; client redirect flashes desktop) тАФ but confirm the actual FREE behaviour before prioritising.** Why MOB-1 didn't solve it: (1) the only redirect is client-side in `AdminLayout` (`innerWidth<768 тЖТ router.replace('/m')`, L86-95) тЖТ it runs ONLY when AdminLayout mounts (APP subdomain), so it does NOTHING on the WORKHUB subdomain (where free mobile lands) + flashes desktop first; (2) the MOB-1 middleware change was only adding `manifest-mobile.json` to the matcher тАФ NO routing; (3) the desktop `manifest.json` is served on `/admin`, so a PWA installed from desktop has `start_url:/admin` тЖТ never reaches `/m`. **`planType` IS in the JWT** (`auth.ts` L205/225) so middleware can gate. **FIX (server-side, in `middleware.ts`):** (a) detect mobile via `user-agent`; (b) read `token.planType`; (c) Branch B (app subdomain): if `planType==='FREE'` + mobile UA + path under `/admin` that HAS an `/m` equivalent (clients/expenses/invoices/quotes/purchases/settings/dashboard) + no `desktop-view` bypass cookie тЖТ `redirect` to the matching `/m` route (BEFORE render, no flash); (d) Branch W (workhub): FREE + mobile тЖТ redirect to `app` subdomain `/m`; (e) routes with NO `/m` equivalent fall through to the (responsive) desktop тАФ do NOT redirect those. **Bypass:** MobileShell's "Desktop view" must set a `desktop-view` COOKIE (not just localStorage) so middleware honours it. Keep the AdminLayout redirect as a fallback. **VERIFY:** log in as a FREE tenant on a phone (and a phone PWA install) тЖТ lands in `/m`, NOT desktop/workhub; "Desktop view" escapes and sticks; PRO/ENT unaffected; desktop FREE unaffected. **Commit:** `MOB-ROUTE: server-side FREE-mobile routing to /m (app + workhub)`.
- **ЁЯФе MOB-FREE тАФ free-tier mobile bug batch (Florin 2026-06-19, testing a FREE account on mobile via Chrome devtools). This IS the launch surface тЖТ HIGH. All on `/m/*`.**
  - **MOB-FREE-1 тАФ no scroll + no horizontal overflow.** `m/settings/page.tsx` has NO scroll container (overflow-y absent) тЖТ can't scroll, content cut off тЖТ add `overflow-y-auto` + proper height. App-wide: prevent ANY horizontal out-of-bounds тАФ `overflow-x-hidden` on the mobile shell, everything STACKS when width exceeds screen (flex-col, flex-wrap, no fixed wide widths/min-widths). **Worst offenders: the invoice + quote engines go horizontally out of bounds on mobile тАФ make their multi-pane/wide-row layouts stack vertically at mobile widths.** (Pairs with MOB-4 padding.) **Commit:** `MOB-FREE-1: settings scroll + no horizontal overflow (stack on mobile)`.

  - **ЁЯСЙ MODAL-HAZE тАФ the open (record) modal is HAZY/unreadable on DESKTOP + mobile (Florin 2026-06-20; coder debugging live). SHARPENED ROOT (Florin's precise observation): on hover the text "descends ~1px and turns SHARP, then goes back up 1px and turns blurry" тЖТ this is a SUB-PIXEL RENDERING bug тАФ the text is sitting on a HALF-PIXEL (fractional) boundary inside a GPU/compositing layer, so it renders blurry; the hover triggers a repaint that snaps it to an integer pixel (sharp), then it reverts. Caused by a compositing layer positioned at a fractional pixel тАФ from a `transform` / `will-change` / `filter` / `backdrop-filter` on the panel OR an ancestor. SUSPECTS to check (in order): (1) residual `transform` left by the entry animation (`animate-in slide-in-from-right` / `zoom-in-95` at L599 тАФ these libs can leave a non-`none` transform at rest тЖТ fractional position); (2) `will-change: transform` / `transform: translateZ(0)` forcing a layer; (3) `transform: translate(-50%,тАж)` centering on an odd-dimension element тЖТ `.5px`; (4) `backdrop-filter`/`filter` on an ancestor of the text. **FIX:** ensure the text-containing panel and its compositing ancestors rest on INTEGER pixels тАФ `transform: none` at rest (clear animation residue / `will-change`), avoid fractional translate centering (use integer offsets or fl\`inset\` + even dimensions), drop `translateZ(0)`/`will-change` where not needed, AND remove the `backdrop-filter` overlays (below). **Confirm via DevTools:** toggling off the panel's `transform`/`filter` (and ancestors') makes text crisp without hover. Original backdrop-filter fix retained: ROOT ALSO involves the `backdrop-filter` repaint/compositing on the overlay/header.** Source: `PageModal` overlay `bg-black/20 dark:bg-black/60 backdrop-blur-sm` (L596) + translucent blurred header `bg-white/80 dark:bg-[#191919]/80 backdrop-blur-md` (L610); the panel (L599) ends up affected by the backdrop-filter compositing. **FIX (robust тАФ `backdrop-filter` is the whole problem):** (a) REMOVE `backdrop-blur` from the modal OVERLAYS app-wide and use a solid dim instead (`bg-black/40`тАУ`/50`, no blur) тАФ eliminates the compositing artifact entirely; (b) make the sticky header SOLID (drop `/80` + `backdrop-blur-md` тЖТ `bg-white dark:bg-[#191919]`); (c) if the blur aesthetic is wanted, instead force the PANEL into its own GPU layer above the blur тАФ `isolation: isolate` + `transform: translateZ(0)` + solid bg (but given the repaint bug, dropping the blur is the reliable choice). Apply to ALL modals using `backdrop-blur` (PageModal, TicketCaptureModal, mobile shell, etc.). **VERIFY on desktop Chrome + iOS Safari:** modal text crisp + stable (no haze, no hover-flicker); backdrop still dims the page. **Commit:** `MODAL-HAZE: drop backdrop-filter overlays (solid dim), crisp modal panel`.
  - **MODAL-LAYOUT тАФ restructure the record (`PageModal`) into a vertical split (Florin 2026-06-20). Do AFTER MODAL-HAZE (fix readability first).** Today the body is ONE scroll column: Properties table (L647) + `BlockEditor` (L954) + "Connected Records" `LinkedRecords` (L969). **NEW layout (desktop):** two columns тАФ **LEFT half = Properties** (the property table + BlockEditor blocks); **RIGHT half = stacked two quadrants:** TOP-RIGHT = **Connected databases** (`LinkedRecords` / relations), BOTTOM-RIGHT (quadrant under the connections) = **Journal entries** for this record. Each pane scrolls independently. **Journal quadrant** uses the existing recordтЖФjournal link (`JournalCard.linkedJournalEntries`, L138) тЖТ list the record's linked journal entries + add/open (ties to EDITOR-3; data path already exists). **RESPONSIVE:** on mobile collapse to a SINGLE column stacked (Properties тЖТ Connected databases тЖТ Journal) тАФ no side-by-side at narrow widths. **VERIFY:** open a record тЖТ left = properties, right-top = connections, right-bottom = its journal entries; on mobile they stack; both engines/desktop look right. **Commit:** `MODAL-LAYOUT: split record modal тАФ properties | connections + journal quadrant`.
  - **тАФ MOB-FREE 2nd BATCH (Florin 2026-06-20, FREE tier, Chrome + Safari iOS) тАФ**

  - **ЁЯСЙ MOBILE-RECORD-MODAL тАФ on mobile, records open the DESKTOP `PageModal` тЖТ "completely faulty" (Florin 2026-06-20). PER-TYPE routing matrix (Florin clarified тАФ NOT all generic):**

## LOCALE тАФ Localization (FOUNDATION, not string-sweep) (v0.3/0.5)
> Principle (Florin): fix the MECHANISM, not each leaked string. The "Creditnota voor 2026-19" on a French doc is not a typo тАФ it's a SYSTEMIC fault: text isn't bound to the document's language, and some text is HARDCODED/stored in one language. Fix foundations.
- **LOCALE-1** ЁЯй╕ ROOT FIX тАФ document/engine text must resolve via `t(key, documentLanguage)`, never hardcoded literals. Measured scale: ~43 hardcoded NL strings across `ClientInvoiceEngine.tsx` (~30) + `ClientQuotationEngine.tsx` (~13), plus untranslated module/option names. Route all of them through the i18n layer keyed by the DOCUMENT's language (NL/FR/EN/RO). One mechanism; the strings follow.
- **LOCALE-2** ЁЯй╕ STORED-TEXT FIX тАФ generated text frozen in one language. Concrete: `ClientInvoiceEngine.tsx:344` stores `betreft: \`Creditnota voor ${invoiceNum}\`` (Dutch) into the record тЖТ renders on a French credit note as-is forever. Fix: store such generated references as a KEY/structured ref resolved at render time in the document language (or generate in the doc language). Audit for other frozen-language stored fields (status labels, auto-betreft, etc.).
- **LOCALE-3** Coverage sweep тАФ AFTER the mechanism (1+2) is solid: ensure NL/FR/EN/RO keys exist for every document/engine string + module/option names. This is the only "detail" pass, and only because there's no choice тАФ keys must exist for the mechanism to resolve. Do NOT hand-fix individual strings before 1+2.
- **LOCALE-4** Leaked variable keys (e.g. `Admin.nav.pages.manualTicket` showing raw) = missing keys surfaced by the mechanism; fixed as part of LOCALE-3 coverage. (was CROSS-2)

## PROFILE тАФ Tenant data stability (v0.1, underpins documents)
- **PROFILE-1** ЁЯЯв DONE тАФ awaiting Florin verify. **Two fixes:** (A) **Stale profile:** engines copied tenant into local state via `useEffect([])` тАФ never re-consumed fresh context. Fixed: deps тЖТ `[tenant]`; `TenantContext` upgraded to state + `refreshTenant()`; all 8 settings pages call `refreshTenant()` after save; `AdminLayout` syncs branding via `tenantProfileUpdated` event. RSC read path (Prisma direct) was never cached тАФ `revalidatePath`/`router.refresh()` always produced fresh data; the bug was downstream consumption. (B) **Language triple-write desync:** `environmentLanguage` was only written to JWT in-memory on `updateSession()` тАФ not persisted to DB until next full JWT refresh; `NEXT_LOCALE` cookie relied on middleware round-trip. Fixed: auth.ts now persists `environmentLanguage` to DB immediately; both desktop + mobile set `NEXT_LOCALE` cookie client-side before navigating; Google OAuth first-login fallback changed from hardcoded `"fr"` to `"nl"` (matches routing.ts default). **Florin verify:** (1) change brand color тЖТ engine shows new color without reload; (2) switch interface language on desktop тЖТ switch device тЖТ same language persists; (3) mobile language switch navigates to correct locale path.

- **PROFILE-2** ЁЯй╕ **PROFILE RESET тАФ branding + document numbering wiped (Florin, ongoing debug 2026-06).** ROOT CAUSE (measured, not stale-load тАФ that was PROFILE-1): the company-info settings widgets **initialize local state to hardcoded fake defaults, then PUT those fields unconditionally on save.** Two offenders, same bug class:
  - `src/app/[locale]/admin/settings/company-info/page.tsx` тАФ `profile` state seeds `invoicePrefix:'INV'`, `invoiceNextNumber:1`, `quotation*`, `creditnote*`, `documentTemplate:'t1'` (lines ~123-162); hydrates from `tenant` only in `useEffect([tenant])` (~168-211); `handleSave`тЖТ`proceedWithSave(profile)` sends the WHOLE `profile` via `JSON.stringify(dataToSave)` (~227-230).
  - `src/components/admin/settings/DocumentTemplatesModule.tsx` тАФ seeds `primaryColor:'#d35400'`, `selectedTemplate:'t1'`, `documentLanguage:'nl'` (~160-162); hydrates in `useEffect([tenant])` (~177-187); `handleSaveSettings` PUTs `brandColor/documentTemplate/documentMode/logoUrl/stationeryUrl` unconditionally (~189-202).
  - **The reset:** if `tenant` (TenantContext) is null/stale at save, or a save fires pre-hydration, the route writes any field present in body (`if (field in body)`), so the DEFAULTS overwrite real DB values тЖТ numbering snaps to INV/1, color to #d35400, template to t1. `refreshTenant()` (PROFILE-1) only fixed display, not this write-back.
  **FUNDAMENTAL FIX (general measure тАФ make it structurally impossible to persist a value you never loaded):**
  1. **No fake defaults in saved state.** Initialize the persisted fields to `null`/undefined (a "not loaded" sentinel), NOT to `'INV'`/`1`/`'#d35400'`/`'t1'`. Apply display defaults ONLY at render (`value={profile.invoicePrefix ?? 'INV'}`), never into the object that gets PUT.
  2. **Gate save on hydration.** Block save + disable the Save button until `tenant` has loaded (`if (!tenant) return;` / `disabled={!tenant || saving}`). A save can never run against un-hydrated state.
  3. **Send only owned + loaded fields.** Each widget PUTs ONLY the fields it owns and that were actually hydrated (skip any still-null). Drop `documentTemplate`/`documentLanguage` from company-info's payload тАФ `DocumentTemplatesModule` owns those; overlapping writers is the smell. (Mirror the tight-partial pattern the other 5 settings pages already use.)
  **VERIFY (Florin):** set numbering to e.g. INV2026/00045 + a brand color + template; hard-reload; reopen company-info BEFORE it fully loads and immediately hit save тЖТ values must NOT reset; cross-check DB. Regression-check: editing only the company name must not touch numbering/branding.

- **PROFILE-3** ЁЯЯв ROOT FIX LANDED тАФ awaiting Florin deploy-verify. **Tenant info not populated into quote/invoice PDFs.** **FIX (commit `61e978a` "widen layout tenant profile select"):** layout server select was MINIMAL тЖТ tenant object starved тЖТ PDF blank. Now selects FULL set (companyName, commercialName, vatNumber, iban, bic, email, street/postalCode/city, logoUrl, brandColor, documentTemplate/Mode, stationery, fonts, documentLanguage, numbering). All 4 PDF build sites read the same tenant object тЖТ fixes every path at once. Combined with earlier fallback-removal: leak closed AND data flows. Planner code-confirmed. **RESIDUAL:** `phone` not populated (not a model field тАФ add to schema or omit, don't hardcode); confirm `InvoicePDFTemplate` fallbacks removed + `QuotationDocumentHeader` L30/32 'Coral Remodeling Pro' not rendered live. **DEPLOY-VERIFY (Florin):** quote+invoice as Coral тЖТ all fields populate; then as a 2nd test tenant тЖТ that tenant's data, ZERO Coral leak (multi-tenant gate). [re-added 3rd time after board clobber 2026-06-08]

On mismatch тЖТ non-blocking banner/toast "New version available тАФ Reload" (optionally auto-reload on next route change). Works in ALL browsers, not just PWA. Throttle so it isn't chatty.
  3. **CROSS-7c тАФ service-worker lifecycle fix (BOTH sw.js + sw-workhub.js).** Versioned cache names (include build id); `install`тЖТ`skipWaiting()`; `activate`тЖТpurge old caches + `clients.claim()`; on `controllerchange`тЖТreload (or hand off to 7b's banner). Call `registration.update()` on focus/interval. This is what actually unsticks the pinned PWA shell. Confirm install scope/`start_url` so an old install isn't pinned to the wrong (ERP vs Workhub) shell.
  4. **CROSS-7d тАФ enable + verify Vercel Skew Protection** (platform layer; complements, doesn't replace 7a-c). Pins a session's requests to the deployment it loaded тЖТ kills mid-session API/asset skew ERRORS. Default-on only for projects created after 2024-11-19; **Coral's project may predate it тАФ check the toggle in Project Settings.** It does NOT refresh a stale PWA shell (that's 7b/7c). [docs: vercel.com/docs/skew-protection]
  5. **CROSS-7e тАФ environment+version badge** (debug aid): small badge showing `environment ┬╖ short-SHA` (non-prod, or superadmin-only) so "which build am I on?" is answerable at a glance тАФ directly prevents today's confusion and protects verification.
  6. **CROSS-7f тАФ icon wiring (assets DONE by Planner; only manifest edit remains).** Planner regenerated a consistent icon set in `public/` from `branding/Coral-New-Logo.svg`: `icon-512.png` (now truly 512, was mislabeled 1024), `icon-192.png`, `apple-touch-icon.png`, NEW `icon-maskable-512.png` (20% safe zone), NEW `favicon.ico` (was 404), NEW `icon.svg` (was referenced 4├Ч but missing). **Coder TODO:** in BOTH `public/manifest.json` + `public/manifest-workhub.json`, split icons into separate `purpose:"any"` (192+512) and `purpose:"maskable"` (`/icon-maskable-512.png`) entries; correct the 512 `sizes` (file is now real 512); add `?v=2` cache-bust on the `src`s. Root cause of the original bug: Chrome read the manifest `any maskable` PNGs (cropped by squircle) while Safari read `apple-touch-icon` тАФ now unified. Verify: reinstall PWA on Chrome тЖТ icon matches Safari, uncropped.
  **Also (separate concern surfaced by the same screenshot):** confirm `activeModules` gating isn't OVER-hiding for enterprise тАФ Coral is enterprise and should see the full module set; the reduced Safari list may be newer code gating modules it shouldn't. Verify against `PLAN_MODULES`.

# тХРтХРтХРтХРтХРтХРтХРтХРтХРтХРтХРтХР DETAILED TASK SPECS тХРтХРтХРтХРтХРтХРтХРтХРтХРтХРтХРтХР

## CROSS-4 тАФ ЁЯУК Peppol credit tracking + unit-economics observability (reseller model)
**State:** тмЬ not-built ┬╖ `develop` ┬╖ target v0.5 (but the METER part should land early тАФ see note)
**Why:** As a reseller, Coral pays e-invoice.be **1 credit per Peppol document, both directions**, tiered **тВм0.18 тЖТ тВм0.05** by total monthly volume across ALL tenants, billed org-level post-pay NET-10. Coral must track this precisely тАФ both to control cost and to price/gate FREE vs PRO on real numbers, not guesses. (Confirmed by e-invoice.be support 2026-06-04.)

### CONFIRMED FACTS (from support reply тАФ use these, don't re-derive)
- Org-level credits, post-pay NET-10. No per-tenant activation/fee/pack.
- **1 credit per Peppol doc, SENT and RECEIVED** (inbound counts).
- Tiered rate by combined monthly volume (Appendix 1 of reseller agreement): **тВм0.18 тЖТ тВм0.05**. Exact breakpoints come from the agreement тАФ Florin to supply the full grid; until then use a CONFIGURABLE tier table, not magic numbers.
- Per-tenant balance/stats endpoint: **`GET https://api.e-invoice.be/api/stats`** (per-tenant via Admin API). Use it as the source of truth to reconcile against our own counts.

### Build тАФ meter тЖТ attribute тЖТ reconcile тЖТ display
1. **Meter every Peppol document at the source** (the one place that already increments `peppolSentThisMonth`/`peppolReceivedThisMonth` in `plan-limits.ts` тАФ extend it). For each sent AND received doc, record an event: `{ tenantId, direction (sent/received), docType, timestamp, creditsConsumed: 1 }`. Persist as history (a `peppol_credit_events` table or equivalent), not just a rolling counter тАФ we need monthly history + audit.
2. **Cost attribution via the tier table.** A configurable `PEPPOL_CREDIT_TIERS` (volume breakpoints тЖТ тВм/credit). Compute cost = credits ├Ч current tier rate, where the tier is determined by **total org volume this month across all tenants combined** (not per-tenant). Show both our cost and (later) what we charge the tenant, to derive margin.
3. **Reconcile against `GET /api/stats`.** Periodically (or on the dashboard's refresh) pull e-invoice.be's authoritative per-tenant stats and compare to our internal counts. Flag drift (our count vs theirs) тАФ protects against silent over/under-billing. e-invoice.be is the billing source of truth; our meter is for real-time visibility + attribution.
4. **Superadmin "Peppol Credits & Cost" dashboard** (extend the existing superadmin Peppol-health panel / TenantsGrid): 
   - Org-wide: total credits this month (sent/received split), current tier rate, projected monthly cost, NET-10 due.
   - Per-tenant: credits consumed (sent/received), attributed cost, last reconcile vs `/api/stats`, drift flag.
   - FREE-tier aggregate: total monthly credit cost of the entire free base (THE number that proves free-forever scales тАФ free users cost ~5 sent + up to 20 received = up to ~25 credits/mo each).
5. **Threshold alerts:** a tenant with abnormal credit burn (e.g. a free tenant far above expected); org approaching a tier breakpoint (so Florin sees volume-discount kick in); reconcile drift beyond tolerance.
6. **Feed pricing/gating:** expose these numbers so FREE caps / PRO overage / pricing are evidence-based. FREE caps already exist (5 sent / 20 received) тАФ surface "this free user cost тВмX this month" against them.

### Premises to measure (Rule 2)
- `[MEASURED тЬЕ]` `plan-limits.ts` already counts peppol sent/received per tenant per month тАФ extend, don't duplicate.
- `[CONFIRMED тЬЕ]` pricing model + `/api/stats` endpoint (support reply).
- `[ASSUMED тЭУ]` exact tier breakpoints тАФ Florin/agreement Appendix 1. Configurable table until supplied.
- `[ASSUMED тЭУ]` `GET /api/stats` response shape тАФ probe it (org key) before building the reconcile.

### Acceptance criteria
- Every Peppol send/receive recorded as a credit event with tenant + direction + timestamp (history retained).
- Cost computed via configurable tier table on combined org volume.
- Superadmin dashboard: org + per-tenant + FREE-aggregate credits/cost; reconcile vs `/api/stats` with drift flag.
- Alerts for abnormal burn / tier breakpoint / drift.
- Tier rates + breakpoints are config, not literals. `tsc`+`lint` green.

### Note on timing
The **meter** (step 1) should land EARLY (cheap, and you want history accumulating from now). The dashboard/reconcile can follow. Split into CROSS-4a (meter) and CROSS-4b (dashboard/reconcile) if running strict one-at-a-time.
